# Android Integration | Offerwall SDK

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

You can download the Sample integration from [GitHub](https://github.com/greedygame/demo-offerwall-android)

Integration video

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-1.-add-this-to-your-build.gradle-file)

1\. Add this to your build.gradle file


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your build.gradle file. Once added, clean build and rebuild the project.

Kotlin Script

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#tab-kotlin-script)

Groovy

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#tab-groovy)

Copy

    implementation("com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.11")

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.11'

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-2.-configure-proguard-rules)

2\. Configure proguard rules


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    
    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    -keep class com.pubscale.caterpillar.analytics.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-initializing-the-offerwall)

3\. Initializing the OfferWall


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.1.-parameters-for-init-call)

**3.1. Parameters for init call:**

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.2.-creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**3.2. Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

Obtain your **PubScale app ID** from the [PubScale Dashboard](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
 by [adding your app and configuring the offerwall.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
 Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#tab-kotlin)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#tab-java)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallConfig = OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
       .setUniqueId("unique_id")
       .setSandboxEnabled(false) //Change this to true to enable sandbox mode
       .build()

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig =
           new OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
                   .setUniqueId("unique_id")
                   .setSandboxEnabled(false) //Change this to true to enable sandbox mode
                   .build();

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setSandboxEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in the sandbox environment

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. This can be used in apps or games where an immersive experience is needed. Default: false

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.3.-making-the-init-call)

**3.3. Making the init call:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#tab-kotlin-1)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#tab-java-1)

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, object : OfferWallInitListener {
       override fun onInitSuccess() {
       }
       override fun onInitFailed(error: InitError) {
       }
    })

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, new OfferWallInitListener() {
       @Override
       public void onInitSuccess() {
    
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onInitFailed(@NonNull InitError error) {
    
       }
    });

Make sure to handle Offerwall init failures properly as the init might fail in scenarios where the PubScale system detects a fraudulent environment.

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-4.-start-the-offerwall)

4\. Start the OfferWall


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#tab-kotlin-2)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#tab-java-2)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallListener = object : OfferWallListener{
    
       override fun onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d("PSOfferwall", "Offer wall showed.")
       }
    
       override fun onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d("PSOfferwall", "Offer wall closed.")
       }
    
       override fun onRewardClaimed(reward: Reward) {
           Log.d("PSOfferwall", "Offer wall reward claimed.")
       }
    
       override fun onFailed(message: String) {
           Log.d("PSOfferwall", "onFailed: $message")
       }
    }                 

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallListener offerWallListener = new OfferWallListener() {
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d("PSOfferwall", "Offer wall showed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d("PSOfferwall", "Offer wall closed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onRewardClaimed(@NonNull Reward reward) {
           Log.d("PSOfferwall", "Offer wall reward claimed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onFailed(@NonNull String message) {
           Log.d("PSOfferwall", "onFailed: " + message);
       }
    };

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#tab-kotlin-3)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#tab-java-3)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener)            

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener);

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

5\. Setup S2S callbacks


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setup the S2S callbacks to get instant updates whenever the user gets the reward. You can use this callback to reward the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/android-integration#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

6\. Test the OfferWall


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

Finally, To test the offerwall, build the application to an actual device. Check if you can launch the Offerwall and get the appropriate callbacks.

# FAQs | Offerwall SDK

How do I create an PubScale Offerwall Placement/How do I get Offerwall App ID?[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/faqs#how-do-i-create-an-pubscale-offerwall-placement-how-do-i-get-offerwall-app-id)

Refer to the content below.

[Setting up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)

How do I show my currency icon on the PubScale Offerwall?[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/faqs#how-do-i-show-my-currency-icon-on-the-pubscale-offerwall)

While setting up the offerwall, you can add an icon for your currency. This icon can also be uploaded later on the app details page after creating the offerwall.

How do I test the Offerwall Integration?[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/faqs#how-do-i-test-the-offerwall-integration)

To test the integration, you can make use of the [sandbox environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
. Sandbox environment will have test offers which are very easy to complete. Upon completion of these offers you will receive S2S postbacks on the configured Sandbox S2S URL.

Contact to your Account Manager or email us at [info@pubscale.com](mailto:info@pubscale.com)

# Sandbox Environment | Offerwall SDK

The Sandbox environment allows you to fully test the integration before releasing your app to production. You can simulate the complete workflow from SDK initialization to receiving callbacks without affecting the live environment.

Your app does not need to be live or published to use the Sandbox environment.

* * *

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#launch-sandbox)

Launch SandBox


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FwrZvgCeUlDm78zCmrR8m%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-16%2520at%25206.10.05%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4aa3c5fd-20f9-414f-977e-0efe3e7e074e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=63f845a1&sv=2)

Launch Sandbox mode

**Launch the Sandbox**: Click **Launch Sandbox** to begin testing your integration.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252F3Zeao4OQxzQ66GukIlNL%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-16%2520at%25206.19.39%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dccb42901-ea57-4fce-9a86-062e433fa173&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=25638c12&sv=2)

Enter an User ID for getting logs

Input a test User ID and click **Go**.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#setting-user-id-during-sdk-initialization)

Setting User ID During SDK Initialization

Android

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#tab-android)

Web

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#tab-web)

API

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#tab-api)

Call `setUniqueId("YOUR_USER_ID")` during SDK initialization.

Set Unique user id by passing a query param`?user_id=YOUR_USER_ID`

In the tracking link provided, Append Unique user id as query param `user_id: YOUR_USER_ID`

> **Important:** The User ID you enter here must be the same as the User ID used in your SDK initialization. This ensures that all events and callbacks are properly linked and you receive the test callback for this user.

* * *

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#enable-sandbox-mode)

Enable Sandbox Mode


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Android

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#tab-android-1)

Web

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#tab-web-1)

API

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#tab-api-1)

Call `setSandboxEnabled(true)` during SDK initialization.

Enable sandbox mode by passing a query param`?sandbox=true`

Get sandbox mode offers by passing the sandbox key in the API body as `sandbox: true`

* * *

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment#system-logs)

System Logs


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FmDBgLVhTO05bWBn3o6Ah%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-17%2520at%25202.59.04%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6d34c3e-9563-41a4-8e5d-2ee6e6b2a56e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bcbeeccb&sv=2)

System logs

**Trigger Events**: Perform actions in your application. Corresponding events will be logged in the **System Logs**.

Resetting the history will clear all offer progress for this user, allowing you to retest offers from the start.

💡 You can configure a **Server-to-Server (S2S) callback** to receive event data directly on your server. Check [Integeration Steps](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)
.

If you are able to see all expected events in the System Logs and receive callbacks correctly during your Sandbox testing, you can be confident that your integration is set up properly and ready for production.

[PreviousPromotions](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/promotions)
[NextSamples](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/samples)

# Promotions | Offerwall SDK

The **Promotions** feature empowers publishers to boost user engagement by offering bonus rewards for completing offers in your app. For example, if an offer typically rewards 100 coins, you can run a promotion to give users 120 coins (or any custom bonus) for a limited time.

Promotions are fully configurable in your PubScale Dashboard under the **Offerwall** section.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/promotions#id-1.-creating-a-promotion)

1\. Creating a Promotion


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to the Offerwall section, open the Overview tab, select your app from the list, then click the Promotion card in your app’s dashboard to view or create promotions. Click **Create Promotion** to get started.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FkRDh67DyShELsB5sb70G%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-20%2520at%25202.59.31%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd202c1ed-5a10-4385-b899-edc2a6d0a85f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f66a3c10&sv=2)

Only one promotion can be active at a time.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/promotions#id-1.1.-promotion-details)

1.1. Promotion Details

Promotion Name

Internal name for your reference (not shown to users)

Promotion Display Name

Name shown to users on the offerwall (e.g., New Year Offer)

Increase Percentage

Enter the percentage by which you want to increase the default offer reward for users (e.g., 20 for +20% bonus, so a 100 coin reward becomes 120 coins).

Date Range

**Set when the promotion should be active** (Start/End date & time, local timezone is auto-applied).

**Note:** The promotion duration must be between 1 and 7 days (minimum 1 day, maximum 7 days).

Targeting

Optionally select target countries to include or exclude

Promotion Banner

(Optional) Upload a banner image to visually highlight your promotion (JPG/PNG, max 1MB)

A live preview will appear in the right pane, instantly reflecting any changes you make.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252FYQNqS9GBqNh2Vf8Hfwzl%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-19%2520at%252012.52.56%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf931623-84a3-4ae7-8ae2-285184ea0bec&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a414ad6&sv=2)

This promotional bonus is provided by you (the publisher) to drive user engagement. The cost of the extra reward will be deducted from your margin, not the advertiser’s.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/promotions#id-2.-how-promotions-work)

2\. How Promotions Work

*   **User View:** Users see the promotion and the increased reward directly in the offerwall, along with your custom banner (if provided).
    
*   **Reward Calculation:** The user receives the base reward _plus_ the promotional bonus. _Example:_ If the base reward is 100 coins and the promotion is +20%, the user gets 120 coins.
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/promotions#id-3.-promotion-scheduling)

3\. Promotion Scheduling

*   **Start Immediately:** The promotion is active as soon as you create it.
    
*   **Start Later:** Set a custom start date and time.
    
*   **End Date:** The promotion automatically ends at your specified date and time.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F95496035-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fx0ylFv11SuG05Xj0pGLn%252Fuploads%252Fl1G2YeB3VXHVtMmFimLn%252FScreenshot%25202025-06-19%2520at%252010.13.30%25E2%2580%25AFAM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb1b6981-d021-4376-b266-7ecae029406e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9fe9fc4a&sv=2)

Promotions Actions (Edit/Enable/Disable)

💡 In the Offerwall > Promotions section, publishers can view all their promotions and easily edit, activate, deactivate any promotion directly from the list.

[PreviousServer-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configuration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)
[NextSandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Welcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK | Offerwall SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F47uqFPZw7HlLBl2j2OyM%2Fblobs%2FISBQsuHhQwZxtdY4gfTy%2Fbanner%25201.jpg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=adb43078&sv=2)

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PubScale Offerwall SDK is an app monetization tool that allows developers to make incremental revenue by asking the user to complete some task in exchange for in-app currency.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2#benefits)

Benefits


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Incremental revenue
    
2.  Monetize non-paying users
    
3.  Improves user retention
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2#features)

Features


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Instant reward offers:** You get offers that give out instant rewards on completion.
    
2.  **Fraud prevention:** Our inbuilt fraud detection and prevention system ensures that all the conversions that happen from the app are legit.
    
3.  **Easy integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done within a few hours.
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2#quick-links)

Quick links


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboard](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [Sample app and code](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/samples)
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2#get-started)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides for you to get set up with our SDK quickly and easily.

# Prerequisites | Offerwall SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/prerequisites/prerequisites#before-starting-the-integration-make-a-quick-check-of-the-things-listed-below)

Before starting the integration, make a quick check of the things listed below:

1.  You have a [PubScale App ID](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding)
     and you have created an offerwall placement
    
2.  Ensure your application builds without any errors BEFORE adding the SDK

# PubScale Onboarding | Offerwall SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#create-an-account)

Create an account

Create an account with PubScale through the dashboard at [https://dashboard.pubscale.com](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#request-offerwall-sdk)

Request Offerwall SDK

The Offerwall SDK is currently released as an invite-only feature on the dashboard. You will have to request your account manager for this feature to be visible in your account after you have signed up on the dashboard.

Once you have the feature enabled, you can proceed with creating an app and the integration flow.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#creating-an-offerwall-unit)

Creating an Offerwall Unit

Once the feature is enabled, you can access it from the side navigation list.

1.  Click on the **Offerwall** item on the navigation list
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F47uqFPZw7HlLBl2j2OyM%2Fblobs%2FrDud3oKkOB5oJPabMBK6%2FGroup%252078578.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b694b1b8&sv=2)

1.  Next, create an Offerwall placement for the app by clicking on the **Create Offerwall** button and create the offerwall unit by providing the required details and config.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F47uqFPZw7HlLBl2j2OyM%2Fblobs%2Fg4IosUeZsrVAcZQEPfLn%2FGroup%252078579.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d6f39cf&sv=2)

1.  Once the Offerwall unit is created, you have to make it Live to start using the Offerwall.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F47uqFPZw7HlLBl2j2OyM%2Fblobs%2F2NaTdnpZTbN0e3CN16by%2FGroup%252078580.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2ca43b28&sv=2)

1.  Additionally, you can also setup S2S callbacks for better security.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F47uqFPZw7HlLBl2j2OyM%2Fblobs%2FhbgNqnP4fZI6jqHnT2ve%2FGroup%252078580%2520%281%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5eb1084c&sv=2)

Copy

    implementation('com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.6-beta2')

Copy

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk#id-2.-clean-build-and-rebuild-the-project)

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk#id-3.-configure-proguard-rules)

3\. Configure proguard rules

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    
    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    -keep class com.pubscale.caterpillar.analytics.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

# Initialize the SDK | Offerwall SDK

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

Parameters for init call:

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-kotlin)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-java)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallConfig = OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
       .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
       .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap) //optional
       .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foreground) //optional
       .setFullscreenEnabled(false) //optional
       .build()

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig =
           new OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
                   .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
                   .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foregroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setFullscreenEnabled(false)//optional
                   .build();

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. Default: false

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#undefined-1)

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#initialize-the-offerwall-sdk)

**Initialize the Offerwall SDK:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-kotlin-1)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-java-1)

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, object : OfferWallInitListener {
       override fun onInitSuccess() {
       }
       override fun onInitFailed(error: InitError) {
       }
    })

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, new OfferWallInitListener() {
       @Override
       public void onInitSuccess() {
    
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onInitFailed(@NonNull InitError error) {
    
       }
    });

OfferWallInitListener is an optional parameter in init() method.

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

[PreviousSetting up the SDK](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk)
[NextStart the OfferWall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/start-the-offerwall)

# Start the OfferWall | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-kotlin)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-java)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallListener = object : OfferWallListener{
    
       override fun onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.")
       }
    
       override fun onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.")
       }
    
       override fun onRewardClaimed(reward: Reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.")
       }
    
       override fun onFailed(message: String) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: $message")
       }
    }                 

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallListener offerWallListener = new OfferWallListener() {
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onRewardClaimed(@NonNull Reward reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onFailed(@NonNull String message) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: " + message);
       }
    };

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-kotlin-1)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-java-1)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener)            

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener);

`packages.add(new PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage());`

# Initialize the SDK | Offerwall SDK

To initialize the SDK, call the PubscaleOfferwall.init() method.

Pass the app API key (generated from the console) as the first parameter of the init method. Make sure to call the init method as soon as your app starts up, ideally in app.js or index.js.

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#optional-parameters)

Optional Parameters:

**user\_id:** Pass your user's id in this field to tag your user. This id will be sent along with the S2S callback. Make sure to call the init function every time the user id changes.

**background\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed as a banner on top of the offer wall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. The background will be black by default.

**appicon\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed in the center on the top banner of the offerwall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. Default value is the app icon.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#initializing-the-sdk)

Initializing the SDK

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Copy

    import {NativeModules, Alert} from 'react-native';
    const {PubscaleOfferwall} = NativeModules;
    
    //initialises the SDK.
    //call init once the user is logged in.
    
    PubscaleOfferwall.init( "APP_ID", {
        "user_id": "test-user", //optional, but require to tag user to offer completion.
        "background_Base64": base64Image,
        "appicon_Base64": app64Image, //optional
    }, () => { //onSuccess Callback
        console.log("success")
    }, (errMsg)=>{ //onFailure Callbacks
        console.log(errMsg)
    })

The SDK Initialization is complete. Learn how to launch the offerwall in the next step.

[PreviousSetting up the SDK](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk)
[NextStart the OfferWall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/start-the-offerwall)

# Start the OfferWall | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `PubscaleOfferwall.launch()` method.

Copy

    PubscaleOfferwall.launch(() => {
        console.log("close"); //onClose
    }, (errMsg) => {
        console.log(errMsg); //onFailure
    });

# IP Whitelist | Offerwall SDK

You can restrict the callbacks to be accepted only from our sever IP address(es). Please whitelist the following IP(s) and regularly check back to find possible changes

Copy

    34.100.236.68
    
    //Last updated at: Jan 23, 2024

# Sandbox Environment | Offerwall SDK

Sandbox environment enables you to test out the integration before you release your app. You will be able to test the complete integration starting from initializing the SDK to getting callbacks.

Also, any changes in the sandbox environment do not affect the production environment.

1.  **Switch to the sandbox environment using the toggle in the dashboard**
    

Switching to the Sandbox environment in the dashboard does not affect your production environment.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F47uqFPZw7HlLBl2j2OyM%2Fblobs%2FPS6FBUhu1PWYHkoFILyh%2FGroup%252078582.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4ba5a012&sv=2)

Sandbox Environment toggle

1.  **Copy the app ID shown for the sandbox environment and use it in the app**
    
2.  **Additionally, you can also configure a different S2S callback for your sandbox environment by clicking on the Configure Callback button in the sandbox environment.**
    

[PreviousIP Whitelist](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)

# S2S Callback Configuration | Offerwall SDK

You can configure the S2S callback for the offerwall in the dashboard inside the Offerwall's overview section.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)

1\. Setup Callback URL

When a user has earned a reward by completing an offer, we fire an HTTP GET request to the provided callback URL. The following query parameters will be part of the request.

Copy

    <callback_url>?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>
          
    //Example http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Query Params

Description

user\_id

The 'unique\_id' set while initializing the SDK.

value

The decimal value of the reward earned by the user.

token

A token that uniquely represents the transaction.

signature

Hash of the above values to verify the request (more info below).

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)

2\. Server Response

Responding to the callback URL with status codes between and including the values 200 to 299 will mark the callback as successfully delivered.

In the event of the server not responding with any of the aforementioned status codes, the request will be **retried 6 times** at different intervals. You can utilize the unique token sent in the request to avoid rewarding the user multiple times for the same callback.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)

3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention

The value sent in the signature parameter can be used to validate the identity of the origin of the request. The value is an MD5 hash of the template below. The secret key is an additional key that will be provided along with the APP API KEY.

Golang

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-golang)

NodeJs

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-nodejs)

Python

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-python)

PHP

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-php)

Copy

    
    template := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s.%d.%s", <secret_key>, <user_id>, <int({value>), <token>)
    hash := toMD5(template)
    
      if hash != {signature} {
            return errors.New("invalid signature")
      }
    
    func toMD5(text string) string {
      algorithm := md5.New()
      algorithm.Write([]byte(text))
      return hex.EncodeToString(algorithm.Sum(nil))
    }
    

Copy

    
    const md5 = require('md5')
      
    const template = `${<secret_key>}.${<user_id>}.${Math.trunc(<value>)}.${<token>}`
    const hash = md5(template)
    
    if(signature != hash) {
        return false
    }
    

Copy

    
    import hashlib
    
    template = '{secret_key}.{user_id}.{value}.{token}'.format(secret_key=<secret_key>,user_id=<user_id>,value=int(<value>),token=<token>)
    hash = hashlib.md5(template.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()
    
    if hash != <signature>:
        return false            
        

Copy

    function calculateHash() {
    	
    	$user = $_GET['user_id'];
    	$token = $_GET['token'];
    	$value = $_GET['value'];
    
    	$template = <secret_key>. "." . $user . "." . (int)$value . "." $token;
    
    	return calculateMD5($template);
    }
    
    function calculateMD5($data) {
    	return hash('md5', $data);
    }
    
    $hash = $_GET['signature'];
    
    if ($hash != calculateHash()) {
    	return false
    }

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#example)

Example

secret\_key = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13` user\_id = `30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD` value = `100.1234` token = `525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

Final format = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13.30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD.100.525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#steps-to-validate-the-value-of-the-hash)

Steps to validate the value of the hash

1.  Concatenate the values in the above format.
    
2.  Make sure to convert the value parameter from decimal to integer.
    
3.  Calculate the MD5 hash of the concatenated value.
    
4.  Build Hex encode of the generated value.
    
5.  Verify if the calculated value is equal to the value sent in the signature parameter.
    

As the value of the secret key will only be known to you and PubScale’s server, the hash cannot be generated by a fraudulent third party.

[PreviousStart the OfferWall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/react-native/start-the-offerwall)
[NextIP Whitelist](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta2/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)

# PubScale Onboarding | Offerwall SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#create-an-account)

Create an account

Create an account with PubScale through the dashboard at [https://dashboard.pubscale.com](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#request-offerwall-sdk)

Request Offerwall SDK

The Offerwall SDK is currently released as an invite-only feature on the dashboard. You will have to request your account manager for this feature to be visible in your account after you have signed up on the dashboard.

Once you have the feature enabled, you can proceed with creating an app and the integration flow.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#creating-an-offerwall-unit)

Creating an Offerwall Unit

Once the feature is enabled, you can access it from the side navigation list.

1.  Click on the **Offerwall** item on the navigation list
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FJRKZiDS1kmUf31Npc1GX%252FGroup%252078578.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D75aa1fef-914d-469c-88d1-9c343a79d13b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5ea54577&sv=2)

1.  Next, create an Offerwall placement for the app by clicking on the **Create Offerwall** button and create the offerwall unit by providing the required details and config.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252F1mnqbBerJIMUTJ4nGlQs%252FGroup%252078579.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2490a4e6-18f5-40dc-81bd-51bfbf7e79db&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1f4c6e0d&sv=2)

1.  Once the Offerwall unit is created, you have to make it Live to start using the Offerwall.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FDYA7VLpYVh07yvNt7R49%252FGroup%252078580.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b1ba07c-c3df-40b7-8f5b-1f6b4950ae78&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f43f874&sv=2)

1.  Additionally, you can also setup S2S callbacks for better security.

# Welcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK | Offerwall SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%2Fblobs%2FhKE0septTPS1i1HmgTdP%2Fbanner%25201.jpg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=75e9a981&sv=2)

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PubScale Offerwall SDK is an app monetization tool that allows developers to make incremental revenue by asking the user to complete some task in exchange for in-app currency.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5#benefits)

Benefits


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Incremental revenue
    
2.  Monetize non-paying users
    
3.  Improves user retention
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5#features)

Features


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Instant reward offers:** You get offers that give out instant rewards on completion.
    
2.  **Fraud prevention:** Our inbuilt fraud detection and prevention system ensures that all the conversions that happen from the app are legit.
    
3.  **Easy integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done within a few hours.
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5#quick-links)

Quick links


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboard](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [Sample app and code](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/samples)
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5#get-started)

Get Started


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides for you to get set up with our SDK quickly and easily.

[📪Prerequisites](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/prerequisites/prerequisites)
[⬇️Native Android](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk)

# Adding the SDK | Offerwall SDK

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/adding-the-sdk#id-1.-add-the-offerwall-unity-plugin-to-your-unity-project)

1\. Add the OfferWall Unity plugin to your Unity project

[Download](https://github.com/GreedyGame/unity-offer_wall_plugin/releases/latest)
 and import the latest version of OfferWall Unity Plugin from GitHub.

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/adding-the-sdk#id-2.-configuring-publishing-settings)

2\. Configuring Publishing Settings

Set the minimum API level to 24 or above and the target API level to 33 or above under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Other Settings

Check Custom Main Gradle template and Custom Gradle Properties Template under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Publishing Settings

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252F7fd3PoDMy8KiaYAWHDmu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db86f09f3-4e60-4de1-8259-ae6462fcdc57&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40910e43&sv=2)

Publishing settings

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/adding-the-sdk#id-3.-force-resolve-dependencies)

3\. Force resolve dependencies

**Force resolve** forces the Package Manager to resolve the project’s packages, reinstalling any altered or missing package and removing extraneous packages.

To Force resolve the dependencies, Goto Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve (if the resolver did not open automatically)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FUzYUObvgE35BpwNoljLm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd15261f-4718-4073-ae62-8839fe558896&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4511d285&sv=2)

# Scene setup | Offerwall SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/scene-setup#id-1.-configuring-prefabs)

1\. Configuring Prefabs

Drag and drop the OfferWall prefab from Assets > OfferWall > Prefabs > OfferWall.prefab in the first scene in your Build Settings.

**Drag and Drop OfferWallButton prefab**

Drag and drop the OfferWallButton prefab from Assets > OfferWall > Prefabs > OfferWallButton.prefab under any canvas game object.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/scene-setup#id-2.-configuring-app-key)

2\. Configuring App Key

Enter your PubScale app ID inside the "App Key" field located on OfferWall prefab.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FjHk3b7lTMWYyUznAAgqs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9c547cf-3c4a-472a-bbeb-5e99100b81c9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=85d4d396&sv=2)

OfferWall prefab

The PubScale app ID is an 8-digit identifier generated during the app creation process within the dashboard.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/scene-setup#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

3\. Test the OfferWall

Finally, To test the offer wall, build the application with the OfferWallDemo scene to an actual device. Check if you can see the “Open OfferWall” button.

Please make sure you have the Android build grade version 4 and above.

# Start the OfferWall | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-kotlin)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-java)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallListener = object : OfferWallListener{
    
       override fun onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.")
       }
    
       override fun onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.")
       }
    
       override fun onRewardClaimed(reward: Reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.")
       }
    
       override fun onFailed(message: String) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: $message")
       }
    }                 

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallListener offerWallListener = new OfferWallListener() {
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onRewardClaimed(@NonNull Reward reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onFailed(@NonNull String message) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: " + message);
       }
    };

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-kotlin-1)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-java-1)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener)            

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener);

4\. Configure proguard rules

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    
    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

# Pre integration checks | Offerwall SDK

1\. Make sure you are using Unity version 2019.4.0f1 or above

2\. Android platform is selected for your Unity project.

3\. Use the App ID from the dashboard to initialize the SDK.

4\. Text Mesh Pro package installed in your Unity project.

5\. The Editor must support Android Gradle version 4.0.1 or above.

6\. Ensure your application builds without any errors before adding the plugin.

[PreviousStart the OfferWall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/start-the-offerwall)
[NextAdding the SDK](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/unity/adding-the-sdk)

# Initialize the SDK | Offerwall SDK

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

Parameters for init call:

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-kotlin)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-java)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallConfig = OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
       .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
       .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap) //optional
       .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foreground) //optional
       .setFullscreenEnabled(false) //optional
       .build()

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig =
           new OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
                   .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
                   .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foregroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setFullscreenEnabled(false)//optional
                   .build();

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. Default: false

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#undefined-1)

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#initialize-the-offerwall-sdk)

**Initialize the Offerwall SDK:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-kotlin-1)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-java-1)

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, object : OfferWallInitListener {
       override fun onInitSuccess() {
       }
       override fun onInitFailed(error: InitError) {
       }
    })

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, new OfferWallInitListener() {
       @Override
       public void onInitSuccess() {
    
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onInitFailed(@NonNull InitError error) {
    
       }
    });

OfferWallInitListener is an optional parameter in init() method.

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

# Initialize the SDK | Offerwall SDK

To initialize the SDK, call the PubscaleOfferwall.init() method.

Pass the app API key (generated from the console) as the first parameter of the init method. Make sure to call the init method as soon as your app starts up, ideally in app.js or index.js.

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#optional-parameters)

Optional Parameters:

**user\_id:** Pass your user's id in this field to tag your user. This id will be sent along with the S2S callback. Make sure to call the init function every time the user id changes.

**background\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed as a banner on top of the offer wall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. The background will be black by default.

**appicon\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed in the center on the top banner of the offerwall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. Default value is the app icon.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#initializing-the-sdk)

Initializing the SDK

Copy

    import {NativeModules, Alert} from 'react-native';
    const {PubscaleOfferwall} = NativeModules;
    
    //initialises the SDK.
    //call init once the user is logged in.
    
    PubscaleOfferwall.init( "APP_ID", {
        "user_id": "test-user", //optional, but require to tag user to offer completion.
        "background_Base64": base64Image,
        "appicon_Base64": app64Image, //optional
    }, () => { //onSuccess Callback
        console.log("success")
    }, (errMsg)=>{ //onFailure Callbacks
        console.log(errMsg)
    })

The SDK Initialization is complete. Learn how to launch the offerwall in the next step.

[PreviousSetting up the SDK](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk)
[NextStart the OfferWall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/v1.0.5/react-native/start-the-offerwall)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Welcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK | Offerwall SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1235736282-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%252Fuploads%252FIQmczo2TwxZ41xb2d8KF%252FGitbook%2520Offerwall.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfbd06600-574c-40dd-817f-115a71ff68b2&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6c85820c&sv=2)

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PubScale Offerwall SDK is an app monetization tool that allows developers to make incremental revenue by asking the user to complete some task in exchange for in-app currency.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9#benefits)

Benefits


--------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Incremental revenue
    
2.  Monetize non-paying users
    
3.  Improves user retention
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9#features)

Features


--------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Instant reward offers:** You get offers that give out instant rewards on completion.
    
2.  **Fraud prevention:** Our inbuilt fraud detection and prevention system ensures that all the conversions that happen from the app are legit.
    
3.  **Easy integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done within a few hours.
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9#quick-links)

Quick links


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboard](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [Sample app and code](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/samples)
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9#get-started)

Get Started


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides for you to get set up with our SDK quickly and easily.

[Android Integration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration)
[React Native](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/react-native)
[Unity](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/unity)
[Web Offerwall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/web-offerwall)
[🦉Server-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configuration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[NextSetting up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

6\. Link the module

Add the following line inside the getPackages() method of MainApplication class.

`packages.add(new PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage());`

# Server-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configuration | Offerwall SDK

You can configure the S2S callback for the offerwall in the dashboard inside the Offerwall's overview section.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)

1\. Setup Callback URL


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When a user has earned a reward by completing an offer, we fire an HTTP GET request to the provided callback URL. The following query parameters will be part of the request.

**Example callback setup:**

**Callback URL set by you:** http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale

**Request sent from us:** HTTP GET http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user\_id=<user\_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Copy

    <callback_url>?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>      
    //Example http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Query Params

Description

user\_id

The 'unique\_id' set while initializing the SDK.

value

The decimal value of the reward earned by the user.

token

A token that uniquely represents the transaction.

signature

Hash of the above values to verify the request (more info below).

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)

2\. Server Response


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Responding to the callback URL with status codes between and including the values 200 to 299 will mark the callback as successfully delivered.

In the event of the server not responding with any of the aforementioned status codes, the request will be **retried 6 times** at different intervals. You can utilize the unique token sent in the request to avoid rewarding the user multiple times for the same callback.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)

3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.1.-hash-validation)

3.1. Hash validation

The value sent in the signature parameter can be used to validate the identity of the origin of the request. The value is an MD5 hash of the template below. The secret key is an additional key that will be provided along with the APP API KEY.

PHP

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#tab-php)

NodeJs

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#tab-nodejs)

Python

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#tab-python)

Golang

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#tab-golang)

Copy

    function calculateHash() {
    	
    	$user = $_GET['user_id'];
    	$token = $_GET['token'];
    	$value = $_GET['value'];
    
    	$template = <secret_key>. "." . $user . "." . (int)$value . "." $token;
    
    	return calculateMD5($template);
    }
    
    function calculateMD5($data) {
    	return hash('md5', $data);
    }
    
    $hash = $_GET['signature'];
    
    if ($hash != calculateHash()) {
    	return false
    }

Copy

    const md5 = require('md5')
      
    const template = `${<secret_key>}.${<user_id>}.${Math.trunc(<value>)}.${<token>}`
    const hash = md5(template)
    
    if(signature != hash) {
        return false
    }
    

Copy

    import hashlib
    
    template = '{secret_key}.{user_id}.{value}.{token}'.format(secret_key=<secret_key>,user_id=<user_id>,value=int(<value>),token=<token>)
    hash = hashlib.md5(template.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()
    
    if hash != <signature>:
        return false            

Copy

    template := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s.%d.%s", <secret_key>, <user_id>, <int({value>), <token>)
    hash := toMD5(template)
    
      if hash != {signature} {
            return errors.New("invalid signature")
      }
    
    func toMD5(text string) string {
      algorithm := md5.New()
      algorithm.Write([]byte(text))
      return hex.EncodeToString(algorithm.Sum(nil))
    }
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#example)

Example

secret\_key = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13` user\_id = `30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD` value = `100.1234` token = `525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

Final format = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13.30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD.100.525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#steps-to-validate-the-value-of-the-hash)

Steps to validate the value of the hash

1.  Concatenate the values in the above format.
    
2.  Make sure to convert the value parameter from decimal to integer.
    
3.  Calculate the MD5 hash of the concatenated value.
    
4.  Build Hex encode of the generated value.
    
5.  Verify if the calculated value is equal to the value sent in the signature parameter.
    

As the value of the secret key will only be known to you and PubScale’s server, the hash cannot be generated by a fraudulent third party.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.2.-ip-whitelisting)

3.2. IP Whitelisting

You can restrict the callbacks to be accepted only from our sever IP address(es). Please whitelist the following IP(s) and regularly check back to find possible changes

Copy

    34.100.236.68
    
    //Last updated at: Jan 23, 2024

[PreviousWeb Offerwall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/web-offerwall)
[NextSandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)

Last updated 7 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Sandbox Environment | Offerwall SDK

Sandbox environment enables you to test out the integration before you release your app. You will be able to test the complete integration starting from initializing the SDK to getting callbacks.

Also, any changes in the sandbox environment do not affect the production environment.

1.  **Switch to the sandbox environment using the toggle in the dashboard**
    

Switching to the Sandbox environment in the dashboard does not affect your production environment.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2FzEnl3z0WO9Wi45B4Jg0m%2FGroup%252078582.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7f57ff3f&sv=2)

Sandbox Environment toggle

1.  **Copy the app ID shown for the sandbox environment and use it in the app**
    
2.  **Additionally, you can also configure a different S2S callback for your sandbox environment by clicking on the Configure Callback button in the sandbox environment.**
    

[PreviousServer-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configuration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)
[NextSamples](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/samples)

Was this helpful?

# Setting up your app | Offerwall SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app#id-1.-create-an-account)

1\. Create an account

Create an account with PubScale through the dashboard at [https://dashboard.pubscale.com](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app#id-2.-creating-an-offerwall-unit)

2\. Creating an Offerwall Unit

Once you have signed in, you can access Offerwall from the side navigation list.

1.  Click on the **Offerwall** item on the navigation list
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2FK5zkwq5a6L9tULQEuu2S%2FGroup%252078578.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=269e7d66&sv=2)

1.  Next, create an Offerwall placement for the app by clicking on the **Create Offerwall** button and create the offerwall unit by providing the required details and config.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2FEg7kFlIY1r6SxaZZf4cd%2FGroup%252078579.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a339a59b&sv=2)

1.  Once the Offerwall unit is created, you have to make it Live to start using the Offerwall.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2F4sia7rIl4kIp4hANnnk8%2FGroup%252078580.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5450486&sv=2)

1.  You can setup S2S callbacks here for better security and instant updates on rewards.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F9dUUmbZ8oNwa2CoHqvab%2Fblobs%2F5BaUpl4HJpReLhU4i3Ka%2FGroup%252078580%2520%281%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6dcd9d5d&sv=2)

[PreviousWelcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9)
[NextAndroid Integration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.9/basic-integration/android-integration)

# IP Whitelist | Offerwall SDK

You can restrict the callbacks to be accepted only from our sever IP address(es). Please whitelist the following IP(s) and regularly check back to find possible changes

Copy

    34.100.236.68
