# Unity | Offerwall SDK

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#preintegration-checks)

[✅](https://www.alt-codes.net/check-mark-symbols.php)
 Preintegration checks


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Make sure you are using Unity version 2019.4.0f1 or above
    
*   Ensure your application builds without any errors before adding the plugin.
    
*   Android platform is selected for your Unity project.
    
*   The Editor must support Android Gradle version 4.0.1 or above.
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-1.-add-the-offerwall-unity-plugin-to-your-unity-project)

**1\. Add the OfferWall Unity plugin to your Unity project**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Download](https://github.com/GreedyGame/unity-offer_wall_plugin/releases/latest)
 and import the latest version of OfferWall Unity Plugin from GitHub.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-publishing-settings)

**2\. Configuring Publishing Settings**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Set the minimum API level to 24 or above and the target API level to 33 or above under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Other Settings
    
*   Make sure you check the below-mentioned checkboxes under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Publishing Settings.
    
    *   **Custom Main Manifest**
        
    *   **Custom Main Gradle Template**
        
    *   **Custom Gradle Settings Template**
        
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2Fs8TJG5WoN6GOK95xrVXr%2FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25201.06.50%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c877c055&sv=2)

Player > Publishing settings

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-3.-configuring-dependencies)

**3\. Configuring dependencies**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Adding `mavenCentral()` as a repository in `settingsTemplate.gradle`

Copy

    pluginManagement {
        repositories {
            **ARTIFACTORYREPOSITORY**
            gradlePluginPortal()
            google()
        }
    }
    
    include ':launcher', ':unityLibrary'
    **INCLUDES**
    
    dependencyResolutionManagement {
        repositoriesMode.set(RepositoriesMode.PREFER_SETTINGS)
        repositories {
            **ARTIFACTORYREPOSITORY**
            google()
            mavenCentral() //<----------------Add this line
            flatDir {
                dirs "${project(':unityLibrary').projectDir}/libs"
            }
        }
    }

Add the below line inside the dependencies block in your mainTemplate.gradle file

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.10'

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-4.-force-resolve-dependencies)

**4\. Force resolve dependencies**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Force resolve** forces the Package Manager to resolve the project’s packages, reinstalling any altered or missing package and removing extraneous packages.

To Force resolve the dependencies, Goto Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve (if the resolver did not open automatically)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FUzYUObvgE35BpwNoljLm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd15261f-4718-4073-ae62-8839fe558896&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c95a673969eca060eea708c9fdc31002608f810ed2f72bebef304fa7c837926b)

Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve

OfferWall does not work in the Editor. Please use a real device to test the integration.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-1.-configuring-prefabs)

5\. Configuring Prefabs


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#drag-and-drop-pubscaleofferwallobject-prefab)

**Drag and Drop** PubScaleOfferwallObject **prefab**

Drag and drop the **PubScaleOfferwallObject prefab** from Assets/OfferWall/Prefab/PubScaleOfferwallObject.prefab in the scene.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key)

6\. Configuring App Key


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enter your PubScale app ID inside the "Pubscale App ID" field located on the PubScaleOfferwallObject.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FRAkMAKtY5aAt8EF1wiit%2FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25202.05.03%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8ef4f07f&sv=2)

Offerwall Prefab

The PubScale App ID is an 8-digit identifier generated during the app creation process within the dashboard. If you need help creating an account/app with us, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-1)

7\. Initialize the SDK


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To launch the OfferWall, call the PubScaleOfferwallClient.Initialize(string userId) function using the instance from PubScaleOfferwallObject prefab.

Copy

    PubScaleOfferwallClient myScriptInstance = GetComponent<PubScaleOfferwallClient>();
    // Check if the script instance is not null
    if (myScriptInstance != null)
    {
        myScriptInstance.InitOfferWall(userId);
    }

Expected params:

1.  userID: A string value that is used to identify the user uniquely in your application. If this value is null, the SDK would internally create a userId for the device.
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-2)

8\. Custom loader background image and foreground image


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2F9ONxn8c6Iiwt5azuVfKt%2FGroup%252078600.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=62d5dc44&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#step-1-custom-loader-background-and-loader-foreground)

**Step 1: Custom loader background and loader foreground**

To use custom background and foreground images for the loading screen replace the **demo\_background\_img and demo\_foreground\_img** file located under Assets/OfferWall/Resources with the image you need.

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#step-2-enable-read-and-write-under-advance-image-settings)

**Step 2: Enable Read and Write under Advance Image settings**

Press the preset button on your imported image and then select the OfferWallTextureImporter preset from the menu and click apply.

If the fields are left empty, the default values will be used:

*   Background: Black image
    
*   Foreground: App icon
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-3)

9\. Set Offerwall Orientation


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, the Offerwall opens in Portrait orientation. If you want to change this behaviour, do the following changes.

Add the below line inside the <application></application> tag in your AndroidManifest.xml file.

Copy

    <activity android:name="com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.ui.OfferWallActivity" android:screenOrientation="landscape" />

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-4)

10\. Handling the SDK callbacks (optional)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To handle the SDK callbacks, subscribe to the events that are made available by the SimpleIntegration script.

Copy

    //Define functions that would be called when the callbacks are given
    void OnSDKInitSuccess() {
        
    }
    
    void OnSDKInitFailed(string message) {
        
    }
    
    void OnOfferwallShowed() {
        
    }
    
    void OnOfferwallClosed() {
        
    }
    
    void OnRewardClaimed(Reward reward) {
        
    }
    
    void OnOfferwallFailed(string message) {
        
    }
    
    //Subscribe to the events
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnSDKInitSuccess += OnSDKInitSuccess;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnSDKInitFailed += OnSDKInitFailed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnOfferwallShowed += OnOfferwallShowed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnOfferwallClosed += OnOfferwallClosed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnRewardClaimed += OnRewardClaimed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnOfferwallFailed += OnOfferwallFailed;

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-2.-configuring-app-key-5)

11\. Launch the OfferWall


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To launch the OfferWall, call the AdvancedIntegration.ShowOfferWall() function using the PubScaleOfferwallAdvanced prefab.

Copy

    PubScaleOfferwallClient myScriptInstance = GetComponent<PubScaleOfferwallClient>();
    // Check if the script instance is not null
    if (myScriptInstance != null)
    {
        myScriptInstance.ShowOfferWall();
    }

Can also be used in onClick of a button:

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FXq8IMGKWfqHj5qJvEYcc%2FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25202.09.42%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c2040ff7&sv=2)

Example usage: Launching Offerwall on click of a button

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

11\. Setup S2S callbacks


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Setup the S2S callbacks to get instant updates whenever the user gets the reward. You can use this callback to reward the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

12\. Test the OfferWall


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

Finally, To test the offerwall, build the application to an actual device. Check if you can launch the Offerwall and get the appropriate callbacks.

# Sandbox Environment | Offerwall SDK

Sandbox environment enables you to test out the integration before you release your app. You will be able to test the complete integration starting from initializing the SDK to getting callbacks.

Also, any changes in the sandbox environment do not affect the production environment.

1.  **Switch to the sandbox environment using the toggle in the dashboard**
    

Switching to the Sandbox environment in the dashboard does not affect your production environment.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FNVTUuXGsGT9Ny3shGvow%2FGroup%252078582.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=10113b5&sv=2)

Sandbox Environment toggle

1.  **Copy the app ID shown for the sandbox environment and use it in the app**
    
2.  **Additionally, you can also configure a different S2S callback for your sandbox environment by clicking on the Configure Callback button in the sandbox environment.**
    

[PreviousServer-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configuration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)
[NextSamples](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/samples)

# Web | Offerwall SDK

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-1.-integration)

1\. Integration


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Before you start**

To set up the PubScale Offerwall, you’ll need to add your app to our platform. Follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit app ID.

You can download the Sample integration from [GitHub](https://github.com/GreedyGame/demo-offerwall-web)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FLswXTxEAv7IAMykYqwhk%2FWow_flow%2520%281%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=16bc2268&sv=2)![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%2Fblobs%2FpZAkfHGAYoKlDM5kK29m%2Fwow_flow_dark.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5b3f2fe3&sv=2)

To integrate the PubScale Offerwall, you need to provide a set of mandatory parameters for proper configuration.

**Parameters**

Parameters

Description

**app\_id** (Required)

This is the unique identifier for your app, required for integration.

**user\_id** (Required)

A unique identifier for each user, required to track their activity on the offerwall. We recommend using a UUID as the user\_id.

**idfa** (Optional)

For iOS integrations Include the **idfa** as a parameter when launching the Web Offerwall. This helps enhance tracking accuracy and plays a key role in fraud prevention.

**ga\_id** (Optional)

For Android integrations Include the **ga\_id** as a parameter when launching the Web Offerwall. This helps enhance tracking accuracy and plays a key role in fraud prevention.

To integrate the PubScale Web Offerwall into your website, you have the following options:

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-1.1.-using-an-iframe)

**1.1. Using an iframe**:

Place the following iframe in your HTML:

Copy

    <iframe id="pubscale-wow-iframe" src="https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id={app_id}&user_id={user_id}"></iframe>

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-1.2.-using-a-direct-link)

**1.2. Using a Direct Link**:

Create a direct link to the PubScale Offerwall using an anchor tag. It is recommended to use an image or button for better user experience:

Copy

    <a href="https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id={app_id}&user_id={user_id}">
      <img src="path_to_your_image.png" alt="PubScale Offerwall">
    </a>

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-1.3.-using-javascript)

**1.3. Using JavaScript:**

Open the offerwall link programmatically using `window.open`. This provides flexibility for custom implementations.

Copy

    const appId = "your_app_id"; // Replace with your app ID
    const userId = "your_user_id"; // Replace with your unique user ID
    const sandbox = true; // A flag to toggle sandbox mode
    const offerwallUrl = `https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id=${appId}&user_id=${userId}&sandbox=${sandbox}`;
    
    window.open(offerwallUrl, '_blank');

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

2\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Set up the Server-to-Server (S2S) callbacks to receive instant updates whenever a user completes an offer and earns a reward. When an offer is completed, our server will send a notification to the configured callback URL. This callback provides the necessary information to process and verify the reward for the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/web#id-3.-test-the-offerwall-1)

3\. Test the OfferWall


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

To ensure your OfferWall integration is working perfectly, follow these steps during the testing phase.

*   Open the web offerwall and verify that all offers are displayed correctly.
    
*   Complete an offer and confirm that a callback is received from PubScale server to your server. For the sandbox environment, ensure the callback URL is configured properly to receive sandbox callbacks.
    
*   Ensure the hashing technique used matches the one specified in the documentation.
    
*   Verify that the reward value received matches the value displayed for the offer.
    
*   Confirm that the callback is received only from PubScale's [whitelisted server IPs](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)
    .
    

While you can use the Web Offerwall in an Android app through a WebView or Custom Chrome Tabs, we have observed better performance and fewer chargebacks when using PubScale's dedicated SDKs. PubScale provides dedicated SDKs for [Android](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/android-integration)
, [React Native](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/react-native)
, and [Unity](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity)
, which offer more secure and efficient integration methods. Please consider using these SDKs for better integration.

[PreviousUnity](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/unity)
[NextiOS](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios)

Last updated 2 months ago

Was this helpful?

# Welcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK | Offerwall SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2FNEZcqIt91K5sUcc4F4p5%2Fbanner%25201.jpg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89fb849c&sv=2)

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PubScale Offerwall SDK is an app monetization tool that allows developers to make incremental revenue by asking the user to complete some task in exchange for in-app currency.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7#benefits)

Benefits


--------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Incremental revenue
    
2.  Monetize non-paying users
    
3.  Improves user retention
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7#features)

Features


--------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Instant reward offers:** You get offers that give out instant rewards on completion.
    
2.  **Fraud prevention:** Our inbuilt fraud detection and prevention system ensures that all the conversions that happen from the app are legit.
    
3.  **Easy integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done within a few hours.
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7#quick-links)

Quick links


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboard](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [Sample app and code](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/samples)
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7#get-started)

Get Started


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides for you to get set up with our SDK quickly and easily.

[📪Prerequisites](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/prerequisites/prerequisites)
[⬇️Native Android](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk)
[⬇️React Native](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk)
[🦉S2S Callback Configuration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration)

# PubScale Onboarding | Offerwall SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#create-an-account)

Create an account

Create an account with PubScale through the dashboard at [https://dashboard.pubscale.com](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#request-offerwall-sdk)

Request Offerwall SDK

The Offerwall SDK is currently released as an invite-only feature on the dashboard. You will have to request your account manager for this feature to be visible in your account after you have signed up on the dashboard.

Once you have the feature enabled, you can proceed with creating an app and the integration flow.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#creating-an-offerwall-unit)

Creating an Offerwall Unit

Once the feature is enabled, you can access it from the side navigation list.

1.  Click on the **Offerwall** item on the navigation list
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2FAf87bVBcwfm91ayPxkmC%2FGroup%252078578.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7033533c&sv=2)

1.  Next, create an Offerwall placement for the app by clicking on the **Create Offerwall** button and create the offerwall unit by providing the required details and config.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2FTm3NjNk68xHulfnhovVu%2FGroup%252078579.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43ba75a1&sv=2)

1.  Once the Offerwall unit is created, you have to make it Live to start using the Offerwall.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2F3FmadD4fhapjKLcvwG1H%2FGroup%252078580.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=89e39252&sv=2)

1.  Additionally, you can also setup S2S callbacks for better security.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2FIT2oXIfOaXZlkY7QEWbz%2FGroup%252078580%2520%281%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=276aaa09&sv=2)

[PreviousPrerequisites](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/prerequisites/prerequisites)
[NextSetting up the SDK](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Launch the offerwall | Offerwall SDK

Add the below code into the widget where you want to launch the offerwall from

Copy

    void launchOfferwall(String appId, String userId) async{
      await launchUrlInCustomTabs(
        Uri.parse("https://wow.pubscale.com/?app_id=${appId}&user_id=${userId}"),
      );
    }
    
    Future<void> launchUrlInCustomTabs(Uri uri) async {
      final theme = Theme.of(context);
      try {
        await launchUrl(
          uri,
          options: LaunchOptions(
            barColor: theme.colorScheme.surface,
            onBarColor: theme.colorScheme.onSurface,
            barFixingEnabled: false,
          ),
        );
      } catch (e) {
          // If the URL launch fails, an exception will be thrown. (For example, if no browser app is installed on the Android device.)
        debugPrint(e.toString());
      }
    }

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/flutter/launch-the-offerwall#launching-the-offerwall)

Launching the Offerwall

To launch the offerwall, simply call the launchOfferwall() method with the pubscale app id and your app's user id as the parameters.

Copy

    launchOfferwall("OFFERWALL_APP_ID", "USER_ID");

[PreviousAdding the dependencies](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/flutter/adding-the-dependencies)
[NextPreintegration Checks](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/preintegration-checks)

# Setting up the SDK | Offerwall SDK

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-1.-add-this-to-your-build.gradle-file)

1\. Add this to your build.gradle file

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your build.gradle file

Kotlin Script

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#tab-kotlin-script)

Groovy

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#tab-groovy)

Copy

    implementation('com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.7')

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.7'

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-2.-clean-build-and-rebuild-the-project)

2\. Clean build and Rebuild the project

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-3.-configure-proguard-rules)

3\. Configure proguard rules

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    -keep class com.pubscale.caterpillar.analytics.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-5.-add-native-module-files)

5\. Add native module files

Add the following files to your android app's module directory.

*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.java](https://storage.googleapis.com/pubscale-offerwall/lib/PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.java)
    
*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage.java](https://storage.googleapis.com/pubscale-offerwall/lib/PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage.java)
    

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-6.-link-the-module)

6\. Link the module

Add the following line inside the getPackages() method of MainApplication class.

`packages.add(new PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage());`

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2FczhHuDSTWk8hwZSMKZM2%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14800036&sv=2)

Adding PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage to React packages

We have setup the SDK in the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

     and you have created an offerwall placement

# Initialize the SDK | Offerwall SDK

To initialize the SDK, call the PubscaleOfferwall.init() method.

Pass the app API key (generated from the console) as the first parameter of the init method. Make sure to call the init method as soon as your app starts up, ideally in app.js or index.js.

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#optional-parameters)

Optional Parameters:

**user\_id:** Pass your user's id in this field to tag your user. This id will be sent along with the S2S callback. Make sure to call the init function every time the user id changes.

**background\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed as a banner on top of the offer wall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. The background will be black by default.

**appicon\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed in the center on the top banner of the offerwall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. Default value is the app icon.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#initializing-the-sdk)

Initializing the SDK

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Copy

    import {NativeModules, Alert} from 'react-native';
    const {PubscaleOfferwall} = NativeModules;
    
    //initialises the SDK.
    //call init once the user is logged in.
    
    PubscaleOfferwall.init( "APP_ID", {
        "user_id": "test-user", //optional, but require to tag user to offer completion.
        "background_Base64": base64Image,
        "appicon_Base64": app64Image, //optional
    }, () => { //onSuccess Callback
        console.log("success")
    }, (errMsg)=>{ //onFailure Callbacks
        console.log(errMsg)
    })

The SDK Initialization is complete. Learn how to launch the offerwall in the next step.

[PreviousSetting up the SDK](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk)
[NextStart the OfferWall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/react-native/start-the-offerwall)

# Direct Link | Offerwall SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/web/direct-link#to-create-a-direct-link-to-pubscale-offerwall-add-an-anchor-tag-in-your-html-that-redirects-to-the-p)

To create a direct link to Pubscale Offerwall, add an anchor tag in your HTML that redirects to the Pubscale Offerwall. It's best to use an image or button rather than a text link for this purpose.

Copy

    <a href="https://wow.pubscale.com?app_id={app_id}&user_id={user_id}">
      <img src="path_to_your_image.png" alt="Pubscale Offerwall"> 
    </a>

Parameter

Required

Comment

app\_id

yes

Get it from the PubScale Dashboard

user\_id

yes

Unique User ID

[PreviousIFrame integration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/web/iframe-integration)
[NextS2S Callback Configuration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration)

# Start the OfferWall | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-kotlin)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-java)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallListener = object : OfferWallListener{
    
       override fun onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.")
       }
    
       override fun onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.")
       }
    
       override fun onRewardClaimed(reward: Reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.")
       }
    
       override fun onFailed(message: String) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: $message")
       }
    }                 

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallListener offerWallListener = new OfferWallListener() {
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onRewardClaimed(@NonNull Reward reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onFailed(@NonNull String message) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: " + message);
       }
    };

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-kotlin-1)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-java-1)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener)            

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener);

# Setting up the SDK | Offerwall SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/setting-up-the-sdk#id-1.-add-the-offerwall-unity-plugin-to-your-unity-project)

**1\. Add the OfferWall Unity plugin to your Unity project**

[Download](https://github.com/GreedyGame/unity-offer_wall_plugin/releases/latest)
 and import the latest version of OfferWall Unity Plugin from GitHub.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/setting-up-the-sdk#id-2.-configuring-publishing-settings)

**2\. Configuring Publishing Settings**

*   Set the minimum API level to 24 or above and the target API level to 33 or above under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Other Settings
    
*   Make sure you check the below-mentioned checkboxes under Edit/ProjectSettings/Player/Publishing Settings.
    
    *   **Custom Main Manifest**
        
    *   **Custom Main Gradle Template**
        
    *   **Custom Gradle Settings Template**
        
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2425324002-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%252Fuploads%252FbhnbN0kpLWTXZNUiquh6%252FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25201.06.50%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f02e2a1-5b1b-414d-8e71-90035f1e1801&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=befc650d&sv=2)

Player > Publishing settings

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/setting-up-the-sdk#id-3.-configuring-dependencies)

**3\. Configuring dependencies**

Adding `mavenCentral()` as a repository in `settingsTemplate.gradle`

Copy

    pluginManagement {
        repositories {
            **ARTIFACTORYREPOSITORY**
            gradlePluginPortal()
            google()
        }
    }
    
    include ':launcher', ':unityLibrary'
    **INCLUDES**
    
    dependencyResolutionManagement {
        repositoriesMode.set(RepositoriesMode.PREFER_SETTINGS)
        repositories {
            **ARTIFACTORYREPOSITORY**
            google()
            mavenCentral() //<----------------Add this line
            flatDir {
                dirs "${project(':unityLibrary').projectDir}/libs"
            }
        }
    }

Add the below line inside the dependencies block in your mainTemplate.gradle file

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.7'

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/setting-up-the-sdk#id-4.-force-resolve-dependencies)

**4\. Force resolve dependencies**

**Force resolve** forces the Package Manager to resolve the project’s packages, reinstalling any altered or missing package and removing extraneous packages.

To Force resolve the dependencies, Goto Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve (if the resolver did not open automatically)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3371507213-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FaUVG0uxfukyc5xCdlEhZ%252Fuploads%252FUzYUObvgE35BpwNoljLm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd15261f-4718-4073-ae62-8839fe558896&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c95a673969eca060eea708c9fdc31002608f810ed2f72bebef304fa7c837926b)

Assets > External Dependency Manager > Android Resolver > Force Resolve

[NextIntegration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration)

# Start the OfferWall | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `PubscaleOfferwall.launch()` method.

Copy

    PubscaleOfferwall.launch(() => {
        console.log("close"); //onClose
    }, (errMsg) => {
        console.log(errMsg); //onFailure
    });

# API | Offerwall SDK

By integrating this API, publishers can seamlessly fetch and display these offers within their own user interface. This allows for the creation of fully native and personalised in-app experiences that align with the app’s design and user flow, enhancing user engagement and improving conversion rates.

Pre-approval from PubScale team is required for the offerwall integration. Please contact your account manager or reach out to support before starting this integration. [Learn More](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/faqs#how-to-approval-for-web-integration)

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#id-1.-authentication)

1\. Authentication


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In order to access offers API. Following Keys need to be generated.

1.  Pub Key (Generated once per publisher)
    
2.  App ID
    

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#app-id)

App-ID

In order to generate an App ID follow this guide for instructions on [how to set up your app](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/setting-up-your-app)
. Once completed, you will receive a unique 8-digit App ID. This will be used as App ID to access the API.

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#pub-key)

Pub-Key

In order the generate a Publisher Key a pre-approval is required. This is a one time approval for a publisher. Please contact account manager for the same.

After your account is approved, you can proceed with the following steps to generate your Publisher API Key.

**When you regenerate the Offerwall API Key, the new key will apply to all apps linked to your account.**

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#steps)

Steps:

1.  Once logged in, you’ll find Settings in the side navigation panel.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252FLzR9y0rl7Ktqmh2mp8M9%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5672c74a-5251-410b-b997-63b0923f68b2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=364ee0ea&sv=2)

1.  Go to the API Key section to generate your Offerwall API key. If you don't see this section, please contact your account manager for enabling access.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252Fvvxyxxm8IhUk6EukFbVo%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D734fde72-9169-4094-8dba-2ee7d627240c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a21ec49e&sv=2)

1.  Navigate to the Offerwall API section to access and create your Offerwall API key.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252F9LbRADkCv47wyFGAK56w%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc5c01bb9-6363-4e37-bbb2-38469aa8a75f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2d6ad453&sv=2)

1.  Please copy the key from the image and paste it into your Offerwall API setup.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4253310960-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FwtFu5cQcg9ZXDSngP2aN%252Fuploads%252FkLx6pyQz5jerPC0XG5O4%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e6db12f-36ad-4005-9fed-d6e897764e38&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8cad21e3&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#id-2.-offers-api)

2\. Offers API:


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#description)

Description:

The API provides a list of offers available for your app, which can be used to display and run offers on your platform.

Offers are cached on our server and refreshed every 5 minutes. We recommend updating your inventory accordingly.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#endpoint)

Endpoint:

Copy

    POST https://api-ow.pubscale.com/v1/offer/api

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#auth)

Auth:

The keys generated in the previous steps must be included in the following headers when making API requests.

These are **Mandatory** for accessing the API.

*   **App-Id** – The unique App ID generated for your app during the setup process.
    
*   **Pub-Key** – The unique key generated for your publisher account during setup. This key is shared across all apps within the same account.
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#example)

Example:

Copy

    curl 'https://api-ow.pubscale.com/v1/offer/api' \
    --header 'App-Id: <Your App ID>' \
    --header 'Pub-Key: <Your Pub Key>' \
    --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
    --data '{
        "page": 1,
        "size": 1000,
        "filt": [\
            {\
                "dim": "offer_type",\
                "match": {\
                    "type": "any",\
                    "value": [\
                        "CPI"\
                    ]\
                }\
            }\
        ]
    }'

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#payload)

Payload:

Body

Required

Type

Description

page

Required

Integer

The `page` field in the Offers API response indicates the current page number and should always be a positive integer.

size

Required

Integer

The `size` field in the Offers API response represents the number of offers returned in that response and should always be a positive integer.

filt

Optional

Array

Contains an array of filters to be applied to the Offers API request to refine the results based on specified criteria.

dim

Optional

String

Specifies the dimension on which the filter is applied. Supported values are `offer_type`, `platform`, and `country`.

match

Optional

Model

Contains details about the filter to be applied, including the values to filter by and the match type used for filtering.

type

Optional

String

Specifies the match type to be used for the filter. Supported values are `any` (matches any of the provided values) and `exact` (requires a single, exact value match).

values

Optional

Array

Contains the values to apply the filter on. Allowed values depend on the specified filter dimension.

Filter Values[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#filter-values)

**Offer Type**:

*   `CPR` – Cost Per Registration
    
*   `CPI` - Cost Per Install
    
*   `CPL` – Cost Per Lead
    
*   `CPC` – Cost Per Click
    
*   `CPE` – Cost Per Engagement
    
*   `CPA` – Cost Per Action
    
*   `APK_INSTALL` – APK-based Install
    
*   `APK_REGISTER` – APK-based Registration
    

**Example Curl:**

Copy

    curl --location 'https://api-dev.sikkaapp.in/v1/offer/api' \
        --header 'App-Id: 77754913' \
        --header 'Pub-Key: 09DAE7FB5D9AA83582DE7703348D8087' \
        --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
        --data '{
                "page": 1,
                "size": 1000,
                "filt": [\
                {\
                    "dim": "offer_type",\
                    "match": {\
                            "type": "any",\
                            "value": [\
                                "CPI","CPA"\
                            ]\
                    }\
                }\
                ]
            }' -v

**Platforms**

*   `ios` – Apple iOS platform
    
*   `android` – Android platform
    
*   `web` – Web-based platform
    

**Example Curl:**

Copy

    curl --location 'https://api-dev.sikkaapp.in/v1/offer/api' \
        --header 'App-Id: 77754913' \
        --header 'Pub-Key: 09DAE7FB5D9AA83582DE7703348D8087' \
        --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
        --data '{
                "page": 1,
                "size": 1000,
                "filt": [\
                {\
                    "dim": "platform",\
                    "match": {\
                            "type": "any",\
                            "value": [\
                                "web","ios","android"\
                            ]\
                    }\
                }\
                ]
            }' -v

**Country**

*   Countries must be specified using the **standard ISO Alpha-2 country codes** (e.g., `US` for United States, `IN` for India, `FR` for France).
    

**Example Curl:**

Copy

    curl --location 'https://api-dev.sikkaapp.in/v1/offer/api' \
        --header 'App-Id: 77754913' \
        --header 'Pub-Key: 09DAE7FB5D9AA83582DE7703348D8087' \
        --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
        --data '{
                "page": 1,
                "size": 1000,
                "filt": [\
                {\
                    "dim": "country",\
                    "match": {\
                            "type": "any",\
                            "value": [\
                                "IN","US"\
                            ]\
                    }\
                }\
                ]
            }' -v

* * *

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#example-response)

Example Response:

Copy

    {
        "offers": [\
            {\
                "id": "973839",\
                "upd_ts": 1745834294,\
                "off_type": "CPI",\
                "s_id": "nova.solitaire.patience.card.games.klondike.free",\
                "name": "Classic Solitaire : Card Game",\
                "lp_url": "https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=nova.solitaire.patience.card.games.klondike.free",\
                "pyt": {\
                    "cur": "USD",\
                    "amt": 0.0325\
                },\
                "inapp_pyt": {\
                    "cur": "Bullets",\
                    "amt": 4.875\
                }\
                "crtvs": {\
                    "ic_url": "https://play-lh.googleusercontent.com/TIogtAtBq22AAHUK8q0nkXVi3KPPssCqIjp2J5JmLLuw8sdStdpeiRsPg1STEIo2ng"\
                },\
                "desc": {\
                    "raw": "Classic Solitaire : Card Game"\
                },\
                "ctg": [\
                    "SINGLE_STEP"\
                ],\
                "gls": [\
                    {\
                        "id": "2710875",\
                        "gl_val": null,\
                        "ttl": "Complete Install and Use The App",\
                        "instr": "1.Click on redeem now.\n2.Install the app.\n3.Use the app.\n4.Explore the app and enjoy.",\
                        "pyt": {\
                            "cur": "USD",\
                            "amt": 0.0325\
                        },\
                        "inapp_pyt": {\
                            "cur": "Bullets",\
                            "amt": 4.875\
                        },\
                        "ord": 1\
                    }\
                ],\
                "trk_url": "https://api-ow.pubscale.com/v2/tracking/click?rid=2710875&app=77754913&user_id={your_user_id}&gaid={gaid_for_android}&idfa={idfa_for_ios}",\
                "geo_tgt": {\
                    "include": [\
                        "AT"\
                    ],\
                    "exclude": []\
                },\
                "os": "android",\
                "metrics": [\
                    {\
                        "m_type": "GLOBAL",\
                        "cr": 80,\
                        "epc": 23.87\
                    }\
                ]\
            }\
        ],
        "total": 1931
    }

Response Details[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#response-details)

Field

Description

`offers`

An array containing the offer details. Each element represents an individual offer.

`id`

A unique identifier for the offer.

`upd_ts`

The timestamp when the offer was last updated (in UNIX timestamp format).

`off_type`

The type of offer (e.g., `CPI` for Cost Per Install, `CPC` for Cost Per Click, etc.).

`s_id`

The unique identifier for the app associated with the offer.

`name`

The name of the app or offer.

`lp_url`

The link to the landing page for the app (usually a store link).

`pyt`

Payment details for the offer. Contains `cur` (currency) and `amt` (amount).

`inapp_pyt`

Displays payout details in the application's currency, with `cur` representing the currency name and `amt` the amount, based on app settings.

`crtvs`

Creatives related to the offer. Contains `ic_url` (URL to the icon image).

`desc`

Description of the offer. Contains `raw` (raw description text).

`ctg`

Categories associated with the offer (e.g., `SINGLE_STEP`). **Possible values**: `SINGLE_STEP`, `MULTI_REWARD`, `DEPOSIT`, `GAMING`, `FINANCE`, `SURVEY`, `NEW`

`gls`

A list of goals for the offer. Each goal has `id`, `gl_val` (value), `ttl` (title), `instr` (instructions), and `pyt` (payment details) and `inapp_yt`(payment in apps currency).

`trk_url`

Tracking URL for tracking user actions like clicks or installs, with placeholders for dynamic user data.

`geo_tgt`

Geographical targeting information. Contains `include` (countries to include) and `exclude` (countries to exclude).

`os`

The operating system platform for the app (e.g., `android`, `ios`).

`total`

The total number of offers available (in this case, `1931` offers).

`metrics`

Contains performance metrics related to the offer, including CR (Conversion Rate) and EPC (Earnings Per Click). Currently, only global values are supported.

* * *

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#id-3.-click-parameters)

3\. Click Parameters:


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use the tracking link provided in the `trk_url` field of each offer in the API response to start sending click events to Pubscale. This tracking link is essential for monitoring user interactions and attributing tasks correctly.

Purpose

The `trk_url` is used to track clicks from users on a particular offer. When a user interacts with an offer, your app or system should trigger this URL with the appropriate parameters.

* * *

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#supported-click-parameters)

Supported Click Parameters

The following query parameters are supported for integration with the tracking URL:

Parameter

Required

Description

`user_id`

Manadatory

The unique identifier of the user who clicks on the offer. This will be included in the callback. Special characters aren't allowed except "\_","@","-" and ".".

`gaid`

Recomended

Google Advertising ID (required for Android users).

`idfa`

Recomended

Identifier for Advertisers (required for iOS users).

`c1-c5`

Optional

Custom parameters can be appended to the tracking URL by the publisher and will be included in the callback for reference. Special characters aren't allowed except "\_","@","-" and "."

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/api#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

4\. Setup Server-to-Server(S2S) callbacks


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This step is manadatory for rewarding users.

Set up the Server-to-Server (S2S) callbacks to receive instant updates whenever a user completes an offer and earns a reward. When an offer is completed, our server will send a notification to the configured callback URL. This callback provides the necessary information to process and verify the reward for the user in your application. [Learn more.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

[PreviousiOS](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/basic-integration/ios)
[NextServer-to-Server (S2S) Callback Configuration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.10/server-to-server-s2s-callback-configuration)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Initialize the SDK | Offerwall SDK

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

Parameters for init call:

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-kotlin)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-java)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallConfig = OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
       .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
       .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap) //optional
       .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foreground) //optional
       .setFullscreenEnabled(false) //optional
       .build()

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig =
           new OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
                   .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
                   .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foregroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setFullscreenEnabled(false)//optional
                   .build();

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. Default: false

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#undefined-1)

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#initialize-the-offerwall-sdk)

**Initialize the Offerwall SDK:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-kotlin-1)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-java-1)

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, object : OfferWallInitListener {
       override fun onInitSuccess() {
       }
       override fun onInitFailed(error: InitError) {
       }
    })

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, new OfferWallInitListener() {
       @Override
       public void onInitSuccess() {
    
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onInitFailed(@NonNull InitError error) {
    
       }
    });

OfferWallInitListener is an optional parameter in init() method.

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

[PreviousSetting up the SDK](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk)
[NextStart the OfferWall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/native-android/start-the-offerwall)

# Preintegration Checks | Offerwall SDK

1.  Make sure you are using Unity version 2019.4.0f1 or above
    
2.  Ensure your application builds without any errors before adding the plugin.
    
3.  Android platform is selected for your Unity project.
    
4.  The Editor must support Android Gradle version 4.0.1 or above.
    

[PreviousLaunch the offerwall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/flutter/launch-the-offerwall)
[NextSetting up the SDK](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/setting-up-the-sdk)

# IFrame integration | Offerwall SDK

# Integration | Offerwall SDK

OfferWall does not work in the Editor. Please use a real device to test the integration.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration#id-1.-configuring-prefabs)

1\. Configuring Prefabs

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration#drag-and-drop-pubscaleofferwallobject-prefab)

**Drag and Drop** PubScaleOfferwallObject **prefab**

Drag and drop the **PubScaleOfferwallObject prefab** from Assets/OfferWall/Prefab/PubScaleOfferwallObject.prefab in the scene.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration#id-2.-configuring-app-key)

2\. Configuring App Key

Enter your PubScale app ID inside the "Pubscale App ID" field located on the PubScaleOfferwallObject.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2425324002-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%252Fuploads%252FlhwkZyv4yxbXtpiHiR8R%252FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25202.05.03%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D840846e7-80a8-4a03-9aad-e55e9b9db68f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a31b9aba&sv=2)

Offerwall Prefab

The PubScale App ID is an 8-digit identifier generated during the app creation process within the dashboard. If you need help creating an account/app with us, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding)
.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration#id-2.-configuring-app-key-1)

3\. Initialize the SDK

To launch the OfferWall, call the PubScaleOfferwallClient.Initialize(string userId) function using the instance from PubScaleOfferwallObject prefab.

Copy

    PubScaleOfferwallClient myScriptInstance = GetComponent<PubScaleOfferwallClient>();
    // Check if the script instance is not null
    if (myScriptInstance != null)
    {
        myScriptInstance.InitOfferWall(userId);
    }

Expected params:

1.  userID: A string value that is used to identify the user uniquely in your application. If this value is null, the SDK would internally create a userId for the device.
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration#id-2.-configuring-app-key-2)

4\. Custom loader background image and foreground image

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2425324002-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%252Fuploads%252FF3IN4OMNQRPGZ3Xisjqa%252FGroup%252078600.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D677fa7df-43db-41d5-865b-9f4a0d0ae238&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2ae2c461&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration#step-1-custom-loader-background-and-loader-foreground)

**Step 1: Custom loader background and loader foreground**

To use custom background and foreground images for the loading screen replace the **demo\_background\_img and demo\_foreground\_img** file located under Assets/OfferWall/Resources with the image you need.

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration#step-2-enable-read-and-write-under-advance-image-settings)

**Step 2: Enable Read and Write under Advance Image settings**

Press the preset button on your imported image and then select the OfferWallTextureImporter preset from the menu and click apply.

If the fields are left empty, the default values will be used:

*   Background: Black image
    
*   Foreground: App icon
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration#id-2.-configuring-app-key-3)

5\. Set Offerwall Orientation

By default, the Offerwall opens in Portrait orientation. If you want to change this behaviour, do the following changes.

Add the below line inside the <application></application> tag in your AndroidManifest.xml file.

Copy

    <activity android:name="com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.ui.OfferWallActivity" android:screenOrientation="landscape" />

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration#id-2.-configuring-app-key-4)

6\. Handling the SDK callbacks (optional)

To handle the SDK callbacks, subscribe to the events that are made available by the SimpleIntegration script.

Copy

    //Define functions that would be called when the callbacks are given
    void OnSDKInitSuccess() {
        
    }
    
    void OnSDKInitFailed(string message) {
        
    }
    
    void OnOfferwallShowed() {
        
    }
    
    void OnOfferwallClosed() {
        
    }
    
    void OnRewardClaimed(Reward reward) {
        
    }
    
    void OnOfferwallFailed(string message) {
        
    }
    
    //Subscribe to the events
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnSDKInitSuccess += OnSDKInitSuccess;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnSDKInitFailed += OnSDKInitFailed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnOfferwallShowed += OnOfferwallShowed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnOfferwallClosed += OnOfferwallClosed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnRewardClaimed += OnRewardClaimed;
    PubScaleOfferwallClient.OnOfferwallFailed += OnOfferwallFailed;

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration#id-2.-configuring-app-key-5)

7\. Launch the OfferWall

To launch the OfferWall, call the AdvancedIntegration.ShowOfferWall() function using the PubScaleOfferwallAdvanced prefab.

Copy

    PubScaleOfferwallClient myScriptInstance = GetComponent<PubScaleOfferwallClient>();
    // Check if the script instance is not null
    if (myScriptInstance != null)
    {
        myScriptInstance.ShowOfferWall();
    }

Can also be used in onClick of a button:

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2425324002-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%252Fuploads%252FBkgMzr5FYDEE8GeLgeha%252FScreenshot%25202024-05-09%2520at%25202.09.42%25E2%2580%25AFPM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da37716ed-c61d-4c22-8352-1312fac39a1e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=54d6fa9e&sv=2)

Example usage: Launching Offerwall on click of a button

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/unity/integration#id-3.-test-the-offerwall)

8\. Test the OfferWall

Please use the sandbox environment for testing purposes to get instant callbacks and rewards. To learn how to enable the Sandbox environment, [click here](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
.

Finally, To test the offer wall, build the application to an actual device. Check if you can launch the Offerwall and get the appropriate callbacks.

# S2S Callback Configuration | Offerwall SDK

You can configure the S2S callback for the offerwall in the dashboard inside the Offerwall's overview section.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)

1\. Setup Callback URL

When a user has earned a reward by completing an offer, we fire an HTTP GET request to the provided callback URL. The following query parameters will be part of the request.

Copy

    <callback_url>?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>
          
    //Example http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Query Params

Description

user\_id

The 'unique\_id' set while initializing the SDK.

value

The decimal value of the reward earned by the user.

token

A token that uniquely represents the transaction.

signature

Hash of the above values to verify the request (more info below).

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)

2\. Server Response

Responding to the callback URL with status codes between and including the values 200 to 299 will mark the callback as successfully delivered.

In the event of the server not responding with any of the aforementioned status codes, the request will be **retried 6 times** at different intervals. You can utilize the unique token sent in the request to avoid rewarding the user multiple times for the same callback.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)

3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention

The value sent in the signature parameter can be used to validate the identity of the origin of the request. The value is an MD5 hash of the template below. The secret key is an additional key that will be provided along with the APP API KEY.

Golang

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-golang)

NodeJs

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-nodejs)

Python

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-python)

PHP

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-php)

Copy

    
    template := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s.%d.%s", <secret_key>, <user_id>, <int({value>), <token>)
    hash := toMD5(template)
    
      if hash != {signature} {
            return errors.New("invalid signature")
      }
    
    func toMD5(text string) string {
      algorithm := md5.New()
      algorithm.Write([]byte(text))
      return hex.EncodeToString(algorithm.Sum(nil))
    }
    

Copy

    
    const md5 = require('md5')
      
    const template = `${<secret_key>}.${<user_id>}.${Math.trunc(<value>)}.${<token>}`
    const hash = md5(template)
    
    if(signature != hash) {
        return false
    }
    

Copy

    
    import hashlib
    
    template = '{secret_key}.{user_id}.{value}.{token}'.format(secret_key=<secret_key>,user_id=<user_id>,value=int(<value>),token=<token>)
    hash = hashlib.md5(template.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()
    
    if hash != <signature>:
        return false            
        

Copy

    function calculateHash() {
    	
    	$user = $_GET['user_id'];
    	$token = $_GET['token'];
    	$value = $_GET['value'];
    
    	$template = <secret_key>. "." . $user . "." . (int)$value . "." $token;
    
    	return calculateMD5($template);
    }
    
    function calculateMD5($data) {
    	return hash('md5', $data);
    }
    
    $hash = $_GET['signature'];
    
    if ($hash != calculateHash()) {
    	return false
    }

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#example)

Example

secret\_key = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13` user\_id = `30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD` value = `100.1234` token = `525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

Final format = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13.30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD.100.525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#steps-to-validate-the-value-of-the-hash)

Steps to validate the value of the hash

1.  Concatenate the values in the above format.
    
2.  Make sure to convert the value parameter from decimal to integer.
    
3.  Calculate the MD5 hash of the concatenated value.
    
4.  Build Hex encode of the generated value.
    
5.  Verify if the calculated value is equal to the value sent in the signature parameter.
    

As the value of the secret key will only be known to you and PubScale’s server, the hash cannot be generated by a fraudulent third party.

[PreviousDirect Link](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/web/direct-link)
[NextIP Whitelist](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.7/s2s-callback-configuration/ip-whitelist)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Sandbox Environment | Offerwall SDK

Sandbox environment enables you to test out the integration before you release your app. You will be able to test the complete integration starting from initializing the SDK to getting callbacks.

Also, any changes in the sandbox environment do not affect the production environment.

1.  **Switch to the sandbox environment using the toggle in the dashboard**
    

Switching to the Sandbox environment in the dashboard does not affect your production environment.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2Fhi3J82Irfk38cjMHFvTF%2Fblobs%2FT8TXDZPpYKMkIdvODezO%2FGroup%252078582.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b9cd6127&sv=2)

Sandbox Environment toggle

1.  **Copy the app ID shown for the sandbox environment and use it in the app**
    
2.  **Additionally, you can also configure a different S2S callback for your sandbox environment by clicking on the Configure Callback button in the sandbox environment.**

# Welcome to Immersive Ads 2 | Immersive Ads SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FyxBpl16VjOO7HQNyNSGd%2Fbanner%25201.jpg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b6207211&sv=2)

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Immersive Ads SDK is a powerful tool that enables developers to seamlessly integrate native ads into their Unity mobile games.

With this SDK, developers can monetize their games by displaying non-intrusive native ads in the game scenes, providing players with an engaging advertising experience.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/#features)

Features


-------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Easy Drag & Drop integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done entirely without touching code.
    
2.  **Native Ad Display Prefabs:** Ready-to-use ad prefabs that dynamically adjust themselves based on different dimensions of ad creatives received from Advertisers.
    
3.  **Boost Revenue:** Earn recurring incremental revenue with a one-time integration process.
    
4.  **Scripting API:** You also have the option of using the Scripting API to trigger ad events from code.
    
5.  **Dynamic Configuration:** Change and fine-tune ad behavior on the go after publishing with our remote config features.
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/#quick-links)

Quick links


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboard](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [SDK Github page](https://github.com/GreedyGame/immersive-ads-unity)
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/#get-started)

Get Started


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides to set up our SDK quickly and easily.

[📪Prerequisites](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/prerequisites/prerequisites)
[⬇️Integration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/adding-the-sdk)

# Prerequisites | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/prerequisites/prerequisites#before-starting-the-sdk-integration-make-a-quick-check-of-the-things-listed-below)

Before starting the SDK integration, make a quick check of the things listed below:

1.  Make sure you are using Unity version **2021.3.10f1 LTS or above**
    
2.  The platform selected for your Unity project is based on the target device
    
3.  You have the GAM App ID or [AdMob app ID](https://admob.google.com/home/)
     and a Google IIG (Immersive in-game) ad unit ID. Make sure the AdMob Unity SDK version is **v9.6.0 or above**
    
4.  You have a [PubScale App ID](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/prerequisites/demand-source-setup)
     for the platform you are targeting (Android / iOS)
    
5.  Ensure your application builds without any errors BEFORE adding the SDK
    

* * *

**GAM DEMAND SET UP WITH PUBSCALE:**

*   Get in touch with your Account Manager to complete the demand setup.
    

**IF YOU HAVE ACCESS TO GOOGLE IMMERSIVE ON ADMOB:**

*   Share the Admob App ID and Admob Google IIG Ad unit ID with your AM
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252FAScf5HnExTyY5KX6zTO4%252FIIG%2520Unit%2520Creation.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3159ee42-7ecc-4a60-9460-b59105bb3c10&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eb9b22de&sv=2)
