# Troubleshoot | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-6ebe3b5a-e6da-4390-b370-a348944ef7e3)

Ad Loading Failed

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FjALWGf7hsVSpDhYTFsLD%2FScreenshot_20240205-145155.jpg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7fde2fb0&sv=2)

1.  Make sure you have added the App ID inside the Google AdMob settings window.
    
2.  In the case of live ad ID (Test mode off), this may happen if there is no fill from the Google server.
    
3.  You may encounter this issue when using Unity Editor Version 2021 or later with AdMob versions 8.x.x. To fix this, ensure that you are building your application with IL2CPP as the scripting backend.
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-75d19063-242b-486e-b874-ed3aeb011c24)

No Impressions

1.  If the screen-space ad unit does not receive impressions
    
    1.  It may be due to a low resize scale. Increase the ad unit’s resize scale to ensure it is visible.
        
    2.  If you’re using Screen space - camera render mode for SS ad unit, instead, you can directly use overlay canvas render mode.
        
    
2.  In dynamic 3D game environments, a world-space ad unit may not receive impressions if it is positioned too far from the camera, partially outside the camera’s viewport, or sized too small. Ensure the ad unit is completely visible, meets viewability pixel requirements, and has an adequate resize scale to satisfy viewing angle and screen coverage criteria.
    

1.  It's important to understand how ad impressions are measured. Impressions are counted based on the IAB's Intrinsic In-Game Advertising Guidelines, which require an ad to meet both a minimum pixel and time-on-screen threshold.
    

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#impression_measurement_standards)

Impression Measurement Industry Standards

The minimum criteria for a viewable ad impression are:

*   **Display Ads**: At least 50% of the ad's pixels are on screen for a continuous period of at least one second.
    
*   **Video Ads**: At least 50% of the ad's pixels are on screen for a continuous period of at least two seconds. This does not need to be the first two seconds of the video.
    

While it can be challenging to follow these guidelines throughout an entire gameplay session, they should be a key consideration when designing specific ad placements that players will encounter during planned moments in your game.

1.  Make sure there is no collider between the main camera and the ad Unit.
    
2.  Make sure the Unity Event system component is present in the scene.
    
3.  If you are instantiating ad prefabs in real-time, try disabling the strip engine code option from the build option.
    
    ![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2Foq3Bvau3IXnG8C8nk3uC%2Ftroubleshooting-1.20b9f76e01fde8dfc365.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ad8fa5d&sv=2)
    

1.  If you have multiple cameras on the scene. There are 2 options to address:
    
    1.  Make sure the camera that is looking toward the ad unit has the highest priority depth value.
        
    2.  Use the [**SetActiveCameraForMeasurement**](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager#static-methods)
         on PubScaleManager to set a specific camera to be used for impression check.
        
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FBw0vh1egsxUOxR04nZHd%2Ftroubleshooting-2.b59384c8cc7c6ab8674a.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=34dc17eb&sv=2)

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-87812b65-8d1a-4fe4-adb0-06debb085501)

Impression but No Click

1.  Make sure there is no collider between the main camera and the ad Unit.
    
2.  For persistent on-screen UI, you can register UI GameObjects that the SDK will ignore as obstructions when the user clicks on an ad in the game to click through using the PubScaleManager [RegisterFriendlyObstruction](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager#static-methods)
     API
    
3.  Make sure the Unity Event system component is present in the scene.
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-87812b65-8d1a-4fe4-adb0-06debb085501-1)

The game audio goes mute when there is a video ad fill

*   Check if Mute Other Audio Source is enabled
    
*   To prevent this behaviour, uncheck Mute Other Audio Sources in Player Settings > Other Settings
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252FZmsT2M1wIjOPCF8HKJJQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D62169d1a-5397-4b39-b1c2-ad348418109d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=70ec3655&sv=2)

[PreviousIntegration Checklist](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist)
[NextImportant Changes](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/important-changes)

# Important Changes | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/important-changes#industry-in-transition)

INDUSTRY IN TRANSITION

*   As the in-game native ads industry matures, the delivery of native ads is changing as well.
    

*   It's moving away from needing to assemble each element of the ad (heading text, logo image, big image, star rating, etc ) on the client side by the developer to the Demand partners providing the composed ad creative image or video ready to display in the game.
    

*   While there is a certain trade-off in creative control in the new direction, it enables better ad measurements, higher revenues due to increased advertiser trust.
    

A majority of the demand in the new version of the SDK will serve ads delivered under the new mechanism and hence will require 2 simple steps for ad display customization.

1.  **Adjust the AD Resize Scale in NativeAdHolder to best fit the Ad within the ad frame**
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252Fj5ugpw3xJYhpkwlrzCAB%252FAD%2520RESIZE.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D488bceff-e44f-43f3-8b99-47672106a3b8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3f36e0ab&sv=2)

Pick a scale factor that fits the ad to the best extent inside the available ad space. Note: You will need to build to device to get test ads and check the size.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252F3Jistba79X345ms9BvyN%252FOverlap%2520Visual%2520Check.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D350d9e4f-8b21-40e4-9c48-586cb2a72c1f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ef239186&sv=2)

1.  **Assign a creative to the ad frame to make it stand out from the rest of the app content.** ![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252FwnpRWMqDYX8uidZAy6KX%252Fad%2520frame%25201.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7bf328b-2795-468c-9a6b-70f3b70d8dbd&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=88ba2235&sv=2) ![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252FNoDMd8WxLLZ4q4dalWJI%252Fad%2520frame%25202.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df25fbfc0-334b-4f02-afe2-2b6bf3bf1add&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=74be316f&sv=2)
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/important-changes#customizations-for-demand-in-old-format)

CUSTOMIZATIONS FOR DEMAND IN OLD FORMAT

*   A section of the demand will still be received in the older format. While it's optional, you can follow the steps provided in the next 3 sections to customize the look of ad display objects, which render demand received in the old format (individual ad elements).
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252FtuwE2SZHHtfdYYp0lUBM%252Fhttps___content.gitbook.com_content_Ti7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um_blobs_ztV66RLxgWzTtHxCA2ZT_Screenshot%2525202023-12-04%252520at%2525208.14.41%252520PM.avif%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8311f167-642a-41b0-85d6-5490cd8f75ba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=996391a3&sv=2)

# Adding the SDK | Immersive Ads SDK

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/adding-the-sdk#id-1.-add-the-google-mobile-a-ds-plugin-to-your-project)

1\. Add the Google Mobile Ads plugin to your project

[Download](https://github.com/googleads/googleads-mobile-unity/releases)
 and import the **Google Mobile Ads** **plugin.**

Note: The SDK supports Ad Mob version **v9.6.0 and upwards**

**2\. Add the PubScale Immersive Ads 2 plugin to your project**

Contact your Account Manager to obtain the SDK package. Import the package into your project.

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/adding-the-sdk#id-3.-force-resolve-dependencies)

3\. Force resolve dependencies

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to link the app in the next step.

# Extra Display Templates | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/extra-display-templates#using-a-single-display-template)

USING A SINGLE DISPLAY TEMPLATE

To use a single display template (for instance MediaLandscapeSimple), do the following in the NativeAdHolder component.

1.  Assign MediaLandscapeSimple to the DEFAULT DISPLAY FORMAT field
    
2.  Uncheck the ADD EXTRA DISPLAY FORMATS field
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FCzdphRKh9J73FMUDk4d1%2FExtra%2520Display%2520Template%25201V2.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ec44ca07&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/extra-display-templates#additional-display-templates)

ADDITIONAL DISPLAY TEMPLATES

The Display Handler Templates used in the default Ad Prefabs are:

1.  MediaLandscapeSimple
    
2.  MediaLandscapeBlur
    
3.  MediaPotrait
    
4.  NonMedia
    

In addition to the above display templates, the SDK provides the following templates:

1.  LogoHeadlineCompact (New! added in 1.4.2)
    
2.  LongHorizontalSimple
    
3.  LongHorizontalSimple2
    
4.  LongVerticalSimple
    
5.  TemplateCombo1
    
    1.  Combo1 Landscape
        
    2.  Combo1 Portrait
        
    
6.  TemplateCombo2
    
    1.  Combo2 Landscape
        
    2.  Combo2 Portrait
        
    
7.  TemplateCombo3
    
    1.  Combo3 Landscape
        
    2.  Combo3 Portrait
        
    

These can be found in the path:

Assets/PubscaleSDK/NativeAds/Prefabs/DisplayTemplates/Dynamic/

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2Fdp6ToilRTywE5kmVSucE%2FLogoCompact.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9bcbc43a&sv=2)

New LogoHeadlineCompact template

Make sure to assign the reference to NativeAdHolder in the CheckLogo script if using this template

TO USE THESE FORMATS:

1.  Drag and drop the Display Template as a child to the SS\_NativeAd or (WS\_NativeAd > Canvas) object
    
2.  If using a Single Template, follow the steps from the section above
    
3.  If using multiple templates
    
    1.  Make sure the ADD EXTRA DISPLAY FORMATS is checked
        
    2.  Remove any display templates that you don't want to use from the Display options array
        
    3.  Add the new display templates to the array for the SDK to pick at runtime depending on the Ad big media aspect ratio
        
    
4.  Assign the Default Display Template
    
5.  Make sure the Status Visualizer is visible!
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FnP9AjlqWa0nasrJWx8u5%2FExtra%2520Display%2520Templates.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bf3c6581&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/extra-display-templates#custom-display-templates-create-your-own-template)

CUSTOM DISPLAY TEMPLATES (CREATE YOUR OWN TEMPLATE)

*   If you create your own Custom Display Template, create a variant for portrait big image media as well.
    
*   This will ensure the Ad unit looks good when the ad's big image media is in Portrait aspect ratio.
    
*   In this case, you have to add your custom display variants to the Display Options array as shown in the steps below
    

1.  Set **\`****ADD EXTRA DISPLAY FORMATS****\`** field to Enabled
    
2.  Remove any default display templates that you don't want to use from the Display options array
    
3.  Add your Custom display templates to the array for the SDK to pick at runtime, depending on the ad's big media aspect ratio
    
4.  Make sure the Status Visualizer is visible
    
5.  Done!
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FzPcTO4yjOWZbsfNxgFvR%2FCustom%2520Display%25201.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=23d6bff7&sv=2)

Custom Display Templates

[PreviousChanging Ad Visuals](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/changing-ad-visuals)
[NextPubScaleManager](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager)

# Ad Object Structure | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/ad-object-structure#a-d-image-components-in-the-admob-native-ad-format)

**AD IMAGE COMPONENTS IN THE ADMOB NATIVE AD FORMAT**

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FIINGv7N4PV2UCHkrnfnT%2FScreenshot_20231201_163049.jpg&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f90ea55&sv=2)

1.  Small icon image (e.g. advertiser logo)
    
2.  The Big image showing the product
    

*   The Ad fill may or may not have a big product image.
    
*   If the big product image is available, it can be of landscape, square, or portrait aspect ratio.
    
*   The SDK handles all these conditions automatically and contains Display Handler Templates for the different cases.
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/ad-object-structure#id-1.1-understanding-the-a-d-display-variants)

1.1 **UNDERSTANDING THE AD DISPLAY VARIANTS**

The Display Handling Templates can be broadly classified under two categories:

1.  MEDIA VIEW TYPES (Ad contains Big Image)
    
    1.  MediaLandscapeSimple
        
    2.  MediaLanscapeBlur
        
    3.  MediaPortrait
        
    
2.  NON MEDIA VIEW (Ad does not contain Big Image)
    
    1.  NonMedia
        
    

* * *

**1.2 STRUCTURE OF THE SDK AD PREFAB**

The structure of SDK's Ad object is shown below:

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FWeQi8tGUojxqMPrfaPkD%2FStructure%2520of%2520Ad%2520object.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1c7ba524&sv=2)

The object hierarchy is similar for both Screen Space (SS\_NativeAd) and World Space (WS\_NativeAd) with minor differences

OBJECT NAME

DESCRIPTION

Placeholder

An image to show before the Ad loads This can also be set to None or 100% transparent to show nothing before the Ad is loaded

MediaViewTypes

Parent for all Display Templates containing Big Image

NonMediaView

Parent for Display Templates without Big Image

StatusVisualiser

A debug tool that indicates impression and click detection status Only displayed with Test ads

* * *

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/ad-object-structure#id-1.3-general-structure-of-display-handler-template-objects)

**1.3 GENERAL STRUCTURE OF DISPLAY HANDLER TEMPLATE OBJECTS**

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FlBFXSyLjOOgz9qPdhwqs%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-03%2520at%252011.44.54%2520PM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=18d6c8b0&sv=2)

The image above shows the object hierarchy of the MediaLandscapeSimple display template. The structure is similar to other templates as well with minor variations.

GameObject NAME

DESCRIPTION

BigImage

Has image component to display Big Product texture

AdIconImageHolder

Background for Ad Icon

AdIconImg

Has image component to display Advertiser Logo icon

CtaStars

Contains child display objects for CTA button and Star Rating

AdChoices AdTag

Google requirements for Ad Compliance

[PreviousImportant Changes](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/important-changes)
[NextChanging Ad Visuals](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/changing-ad-visuals)

---

# Changing Ad Visuals | Immersive Ads SDK

Customizing the look of the ads is as simple as switching out image assets on specific game objects in the hierarchy and changing the text and image colors. Additionally, you may also reposition and resize some of the UI elements.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2F0e2kiboOovDDCFTwVZVO%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25209.29.36%2520AM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=68919269&sv=2)

MediaLandscapeSimple

For this example, we consider the MediaLandscapeSimple display handler template. The steps discussed will apply to all other display templates as well.

**CHANGING IMAGE ASSETS**

The starting point of changing the look of the ad is by changing the ad background. This can be done by changing the source image of the Image component on the Display Template root object.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FPU5EIphP2DmMNTtk6N5a%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25209.45.46%2520AM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fd95e76a&sv=2)

Let's consider a Game with a Starry Night visual theme

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2F2GhASDVJfeSewT3kKU8y%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25209.48.43%2520AM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ca7fee53&sv=2)

After changing the Ad background, we can change the source images on certain child objects to further customize the look of the ad.

OBJ NAME

CHANGE ?

COMMENTS

BigImg

No

This gets assigned at runtime by the Advertiser Large image asset

AdIconImg

No

This gets assigned at runtime by the Advertiser Icon image asset

ButtonCta

Yes

You can use the button UI asset from the game here

AdTag

Yes

You can also switch out the default ad tag with your custom AdTag asset

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FAPkjINrlBfxm8jP79Dle%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%252010.15.12%2520AM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fbda7c50&sv=2)

There could be other image objects in the ad display hierarchy, which serve only an aesthetic purpose and can be customized. An example of such an object would be the lower rectangle panel in the above image which groups the logo, headline, rating, and CTA button.

**CHANGING COLORS**

In addition to colors on the image component, the text colors can be changed as per the colors in your game

OBJ NAME

CHANGE?

COMMENTS

AdHeadlineTxt

Yes

Found in all Display Templates as it is a required field

AdCtaTxt

Yes

Found in all Display Templates as it is a required field

BodyTxt

Yes

Is an optional field. Not present in all Display Templates.

StarTypeTxt

Yes

Is an optional field

BigImg

No

Will be set to white at runtime to preserve the look of the Large image provided by the Advertiser

AdIconImg

No

Will be set to white at runtime to preserve the look of the Small Icon image provided by the Advertiser

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FQZjQS9Qtofg4OAwgf7Uj%2Fg5.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d911da0b&sv=2)

\*NOTE: The Logo and Large Product Image on the right are SAMPLES for illustration purposes

* * *

And that's all there is to customize the look of an Ad Display Template.

You can go ahead and customize other Display Templates as well - MediaLandscapeBlur, MediaPotrait, and NonMedia. The same steps apply with minor variations.

Here's an example of the ad in a game with wooden visual theme:

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FFWigHvPUKsT6HIUaf3ra%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25202.36.56%2520PM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6f3a5c23&sv=2)

In addition to this, you can adjust the position of individual elements by changing values in the RectTransform and the built-in Unity UI Layout components.

* * *

CHANGING AD SIZE:

The Ad size can be changed by adjusting the Rect Transform scale.

The important pointer to keep in mind is to make sure the scaling is uniform (Same values for X and Y)

CHANGING AD SHAPE:

You can change the Ad Shape by changing the width and height value of the Rect Transform on the Root Object (SS\_NativeAd or WS\_NativeAd)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FwLnGIKPpyCtjcoDkPwJZ%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25204.58.51%2520PM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7eb4533&sv=2)

This will impact both MediaType as well NonMediaType display templates

If you want to change only one of these categories, then instead of the Root object you can adjust the Left, Right, Top, and Bottom padding values on the MediaType or NonMediaType objects.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FztV66RLxgWzTtHxCA2ZT%2FScreenshot%25202023-12-04%2520at%25208.14.41%2520PM.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3e6cac54&sv=2)

In this case, you could disable the Image component on the root game object (SS\_NativeAd or WS\_NativeAd) to remove the light gray background.

Once new values are set, you may need to adjust the properties on certain child elements depending on the structure of the Display template. Make sure to test adjusted values across different display resolutions

[PreviousAd Object Structure](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/ad-object-structure)
[NextExtra Display Templates](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/extra-display-templates)

# Scene setup | Immersive Ads SDK

**1\. Configure PubScaleManager prefab**

Drag and drop the PubScaleManager prefab from **Assets/PubscaleSDK/Common/Prefabs/PubScaleManager.prefab** in the first scene in your Build Settings.

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/scene-setup#id-2.-drag-and-drop-native-a-d-unit-prefab)

2\. Drag and Drop Native Ad Unit prefab

Drag and drop any of the Native ad unit prefab from the path Assets > PubScaleSDK > NativeAds > Prefabs > AdHolderUnits into your gameplay scene.

If using any prefab from the “ScreenSpaceCamera” folder, then put it under a Canvas using **Screen Space-Camera** render or **Overlay render mode.**

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/scene-setup#id-3.-configuring-default-a-d-unit)

3\. Configuring Default Ad Unit

Open the Settings Tab in the PubScale Main Menu found under **Window > PubScale SDK > Main** and Enter the Native Ads settings. Add Native Ad IDs in the Fallback Native ID field.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2F5dzp65ACN6VynDWecimp%2FFallbackID.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c5d08c2a&sv=2)

Android Native ads settings

Adding Native Ad IDs in the Fallback Native ID field will ensure ads are requested in case there is a network delay in receiving the dynamic ad config file from the server.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252FyjJcZdRoVV5j9I5JV1Uq%252FAndroid%2520Settings%2520500x360.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D477891a3-a752-45a8-8831-96a5bf00e203&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71d2a1c1&sv=2)

Android Platform

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252F9005NDdvBmbKoOWeLnyU%252FiOS%2520Settings%2520500x360.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81a787a8-80a9-4382-9d36-474c35cdf9ba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2a2b7466&sv=2)

iOS Platform

1.  **Assign Unique Ad Tag for Ad Units**
    

Ensure each ad unit has a unique Ad Tag assigned. Example: Home\_Screen\_Unit or level\_fail\_ad\_unit. This allows us to analyze the performance of each ad unit for further optimization.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2F93cFPzJ9Aku66yPUvW73%2FAdTag.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94060541&sv=2)

We have now completed setting up the ads. Let's proceed to the next step to learn how to test the ads.

[PreviousApp Linking](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/app-linking)
[NextTesting the integration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/testing-the-integration)

Last updated 11 days ago

# Testing the integration | Immersive Ads SDK

To test the integration, always check the **Use Test Mode** **field in the** PubScale Editor window. This will enable test ads and show a debug UI over the native ad for checking Ad Impressions and Clicks.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252FvzPzHJInjfNLIaAszcqe%252FAndroid%2520Settings%2520500x360%2520Test%2520Mode.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D85d0f4cb-b3ae-45fe-9a63-d848db289d4d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=648a37e7&sv=2)

**PubScale Dummy test ads**

Hit the play button in the editor and ensure PubScale dummy test ads are visible and there are no errors or warnings.

The impressions and clicks do not work inside the Editor.

**Test Impressions and clicks**

Finally, to test Impressions and Clicks, **build the application on an actual device****.** Check if you can see the impression indicator turning green when the ad comes inside the camera view, and the click indicator turning green when you tap on the ad.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252FYmRHy3dCWWYr7uSqz68K%252FTest%2520Ad%25201.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D995b727b-547a-437e-b11c-1fdbd690e4e9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aa75c3eb&sv=2)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2403784804-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%252Fuploads%252FZsMphzVyEvXQyaiumhYa%252FTest%2520Ad%25202.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ded8ba40c-a55a-4250-ad26-f1407c3c2348&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d66c2a3d&sv=2)

# PubScaleManager | Immersive Ads SDK

The PubScaleManager handles initialization and all the requests and response caching for ads. It is a singleton component that can be accessed from anywhere. Native ads won't work if this component is missing from the scene.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager#properties)

Properties

Name

Description

**IsInitialized**

Use to check if the PubScale SDK is initialized

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager#static-methods)

Static Methods

Name

Description

SetActiveCameraForMeasurement

By default, the SDK uses the camera with the highest depth for measurement. In scenes with multiple cameras, this default camera might not be the one rendering the primary game screen from the player's perspective.

If the wrong camera is used for measurement, the SDK cannot determine if the ad is viewable, which prevents impressions from being reported. It can also cause the ad to be unclickable.

Use this method to explicitly set the camera that is aligned with the player's view

SetSdkToRemoveAdsPurchasedForThisSession

Use this API to adjust SDKs behaviour when Remove Ads IAP is active for a session. The SDK does not persist this information as Remove Ads can be permanent or part of a time based subscription. This API needs to be set on app open every session when RemoveAds is active

RegisterFriendlyObstruction

You can register up to 2 UI GameObjects that the SDK will ignore as obstructions when the user clicks on an ad in the game with the intention of clicking through. A friendly UI object example could be a virtual joystick that appears on the screen wherever the user taps.

UnRegisterFriendlyObstruction

Use this method to un-register a UI gameobject previously registered as a friendly object.

[PreviousExtra Display Templates](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/presentation/extra-display-templates)
[NextNativeAdHolder](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/nativeadholder)

Last updated 11 days ago

# Integration Checklist | Immersive Ads SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#basic-checks)

Basic Checks:

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#id-1.-replace-the-pubscale-placeholder)

1\. **Replace the PubScale Placeholder**

It is important that you replace the PubScale placeholder with your game’s assets, which is displayed when there's no ad available.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FG2u9FOPdgAkL7yrdFDsc%2FPlaceholder1.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d1a7f001&sv=2)

2\. **Assign Unique Ad Tag for Ad Units**

Ensure each ad unit has a unique Ad Tag assigned. Example: Home\_Screen\_Unit or level\_fail\_ad\_unit. This allows us to analyze the performance of each ad unit for further optimization.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2F93cFPzJ9Aku66yPUvW73%2FAdTag.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=94060541&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#visual-checks)

Visual Checks:

1\. **Avoid Ad Unit Overlap with Screen Elements**

Ensure ad units do not overlap with other on-screen elements.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FEDNTcMZ1XXcTjFIzqaUr%2FAdUnit%2520Overlap.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a44ebc1d&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#functional-checks)

Functional Checks:

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#id-1.-ensure-impressions-and-clicks-are-registered)

1\. **Ensure Impressions and Clicks are registered**

Build the application to an actual device. Verify if the impression indicator turns green when the ad is in the camera view and if the click indicator turns green when you tap on the ad.

If the Impression indicator is not green, [find the fix here.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-75d19063-242b-486e-b874-ed3aeb011c24)

If the Click indicator is not green, [find the fix here.](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot#id-87812b65-8d1a-4fe4-adb0-06debb085501)

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FVmtwj0ewNFKGdBtk2zZg%2Fclick%2520check.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e20ec073&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#id-2.-disable-a-d-unit-during-popups-and-overlays)

2\. **Disable Ad unit During Popups and Overlays**

Ensure that when a popup or overlay appears over an ad unit, the background ad unit is disabled to prevent accidental clicks, avoiding potential policy issues due to high CTR.

To disable the ad, call HideAd() on nativeAdHolder, and to enable it again use UnHideAd()

Ensure the ad unit is disabled even when it's completely hidden by the overlay.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FSTTy7O0TvAaHvl59xlAs%2FAdUnit%2520Overlay.gif&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f9ce3b6d&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#id-3.-enable-status-visualizer)

3\. **Enable Status Visualizer:**

Before sending a build to our QA for testing, ensure the Status Visualizer is enabled.

**You don't need to disable it;** **it will be automatically hidden** when Test Mode is disabled in PubScale Settings.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FnceAkQHWZnN9qosoaqLi%2FStatusVisualizer.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5b927090&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/integration-checklist#id-4.-a-d-request-management)

4\. **Ad Request Management:**

**To Allow Subsequent Ad Requests:**

This is to be done only if your ad is placed on **panels or pop-ups**

If your ad is placed on panels or popups, disable AutoFetch() and manually call FetchAd() only when the UI panel or overlay is active.

When fetching an ad manually, include a counter. If it has been over 15 seconds since the last ad impression, fetch a new one; otherwise, continue showing the current ad.

Subscribing to Event\_OnAdLoaded on NativeAdHolder records the last ad load time. This prevents multiple ad requests, especially during frequent panel openings and closings.

**Avoid Ad Unit Triggering Multiple Requests:**

To address this issue, ensure that AutoFetch() is disabled whenever FetchAd() is called manually.

**5\. Rollout with A/B Test**

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FTi7L0s0VAeOE03JAn3Um%2Fblobs%2FDBsoKvug6B39kltHKadK%2F165_benefits_AB_testing_illustration_blog.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4092e0ef&sv=2)

If you plan to roll out with an A/B test where ads are shown to some of the users while others don't see them, make sure to follow the steps below:

1.  The first step would be to **remove the PubScaleManager prefab from the first scene**
    
2.  Once a response is received from the A/B test service (such as Firebase Remote config)
    
    1.  If the user is to be shown ads, you can instantiate PubScaleManager like any GameObject or it can also be loaded from the Resources folder
        
    2.  Once the PubScaleManager is instantiated, it will begin Caching Ads
        
    
3.  In addition to the above, the **default state of all Native ad Game Objects needs to be Disabled.** Otherwise, when the native ad object requests an ad, the PubScaleManager will get dynamically instantiated (lazy loaded) and begin caching ads.
    

The main goal is to prevent the PubScaleManager from being loaded for users who are not supposed to see ads. If active, it will cache ads that will not get shown, impacting Show Rate negatively driving down ecpm.

Doing the above steps (2) and (3) ensures the A/B test happens correctly.

[PreviousTesting the integration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/testing-the-integration)
[NextTroubleshoot](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/integration/troubleshoot)

Last updated 18 hours ago

# NativeAdHolder | Immersive Ads SDK

Native Ad Holders communicate with the PubScaleManager to send ad requests and receive ad fills. It is the packaging unit of a single native ad placement in your scene and handles how and when to make Ad requests.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/nativeadholder#properties)

Properties:

Name

Description

**AdResizeScale**

Allows adjusting the ad scale to find the optimal fit inside the available space for the ad

**adTag**

This tag is used to identify an Ad placement in your game to track log events. Make sure they are unique.

**canvas**

Reference to the parent canvas component.

**placeholder**

This game object will be shown before the Ad loads and will get disabled once the ad is loaded.

**adDisplay**

Reference to the default [NativeAdDisplayHandler](https://github.com/GreedyGame/sdkone-unity_native_ads_plugin/wiki/NativeAdDisplayHandler)
 component which will determine how the native ad is shown once it is loaded.

MORE FORMATS (Optional)

You can add more display variations. At runtime, the plugin selects the best variant based on the ad received.

**landscapeAdFormats**

List of NativeAdDisplayHandlers tailored for Ads with a Landscape product image.

**portraitAdFormats**

List of NativeAdDisplayHandler tailored for Ads with a Portrait product image.

**nonMediaType**

List of NativeAdDisplayHandler which handles cases when the advertisement does not have a product image.

**UseExtraFormats**

Boolean that tells the SDK to search the extra landscape and portrait formats at runtime when set to true. Otherwise, it will use only the default format assigned to adDisplay field.

**AD FETCH OPTIONS**

**AutoFetch**

If enabled, the Ad will automatically be requested in OnEnable for the Game Object

**TriggerFetchWithCollider**

If enabled, the Ad request will be made when a collider with a certain tag enters inside the bounds of the attached collider component. Make sure the IsTrigger is checked for the collider

**TriggerOnCollisionWithTag**

The game object Tag that will trigger the Ad request if TriggerFetchWithCollider is enabled

If both the above are deselected, the Ad Holder expects you to invoke FetchAd() manually from another script

**RefreshRate**

The Native Ad Holder makes a new ad request using this delay value after an impression is registered on the current ad displayed. The recommended value is 30s after an impression.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/nativeadholder#public-methods)

Public Methods:

All these methods can be overloaded

Name

Description

**FetchAd**

Generates request for a new Ad.

**HideAd**

(⚠️ Native Ads can register click events even if they are overlapped by other UI components.) The AdDisplayHandler is disabled, and the placeholder object is activated. This prevents the ad from registering an unintentional click.

**UnHideAd**

Re-show the ad once the overlapping UI is not active

**StopRefresh**

Stops the Ad unit refresh calls.

**ResetTriggerByColliderAdFetchCondition**

Resets the condition to trigger a FetchAd call when using Collider as trigger

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/nativeadholder#events)

Events

Name

Description

**Event\_AdRequest**

The event is raised before the referenced **NativeAdHolder** component requests a new Ad from the ad cache.

**Event\_OnNativeAdActive**

This static event is raised when any **NativeAdHolder** component gets activated in the scene.

**Event\_OnAdLoaded**

The event is raised when the referenced **NativeAdHolder** component receives its Ad fill from the ad cache.

**Event\_OnAdFillNotReceivedInThisAttempt**

The event is raised when there is no ad present in the cache at the time of the request by the NativeAdHolder

**Event\_OnAdImpression**

The event is raised when the referenced **NativeAdHolder** component registers an impression for the loaded Ad.

**Event\_OnAdClicked**

The event is raised when the referenced **NativeAdHolder** component registers a click for the active Ad.

**Event\_OnAdValuePaid**

The event is raised when the impression-level revenue is available for the current impression.

*   Please make sure to subscribe to Event\_AdRequest in the Awake() callback in order not to miss the Auto-Fetch **Event\_AdRequest,** which is triggered in OnEnable()
    

[PreviousPubScaleManager](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/scripting-api/pubscalemanager)
[NextSamples](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/immersive-ads-sdk/samples)

# Welcome to PubScale Offerwall SDK | Offerwall SDK

![Page cover](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcJjYVtSXK83YJkG3H9nv%2Fblobs%2FUbivQhqP2zLnd4mbqOcS%2Fbanner%25201.jpg&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fd41d9e9&sv=2)

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The PubScale Offerwall SDK is an app monetization tool that allows developers to make incremental revenue by asking the user to complete some task in exchange for in-app currency.

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1#benefits)

Benefits


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Incremental revenue
    
2.  Monetize non-paying users
    
3.  Improves user retention
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1#features)

Features


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Instant reward offers:** You get offers that give out instant rewards on completion.
    
2.  **Fraud prevention:** Our inbuilt fraud detection and prevention system ensures that all the conversions that happen from the app are legit.
    
3.  **Easy integration:** The SDK provides a straightforward integration process, and can be done within a few hours.
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1#quick-links)

Quick links


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  [PubScale dashboard](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)
    
2.  [Sample app and code](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/samples)
    

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1#get-started)

Get Started


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We've put together some helpful guides for you to get set up with our SDK quickly and easily.

[📪Prerequisites](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/prerequisites/prerequisites)
[⬇️Native Android](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk)
[⬇️React Native](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk)
[🦉S2S Callback Configuration](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration)

[NextPrerequisites](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/prerequisites/prerequisites)

# PubScale Onboarding | Offerwall SDK

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#create-an-account)

Create an account

Create an account with PubScale through the dashboard at [https://dashboard.pubscale.com](https://dashboard.pubscale.com/)

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#request-offerwall-sdk)

Request Offerwall SDK

The Offerwall SDK is currently released as an invite-only feature on the dashboard. You will have to request your account manager for this feature to be visible in your account after you have signed up on the dashboard.

Once you have the feature enabled, you can proceed with creating an app and the integration flow.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/prerequisites/pubscale-onboarding#creating-an-offerwall-unit)

Creating an Offerwall Unit

Once the feature is enabled, you can access it from the side navigation list.

1.  Click on the **Offerwall** item on the navigation list
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcJjYVtSXK83YJkG3H9nv%2Fblobs%2FDRLg1dxyz9dJ5WGcGyHz%2FGroup%252078578.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98f38367&sv=2)

1.  Next, create an Offerwall placement for the app by clicking on the **Create Offerwall** button and create the offerwall unit by providing the required details and config.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcJjYVtSXK83YJkG3H9nv%2Fblobs%2FbliloCVCkrIVts2GMwCZ%2FGroup%252078579.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d383a6c1&sv=2)

1.  Once the Offerwall unit is created, you have to make it Live to start using the Offerwall.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcJjYVtSXK83YJkG3H9nv%2Fblobs%2F69joWvJGPSV2KVXjF7VF%2FGroup%252078580.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36d6fc0f&sv=2)

1.  Additionally, you can also setup S2S callbacks for better security.
    

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcJjYVtSXK83YJkG3H9nv%2Fblobs%2Fryrqc5cEmK0fM0VVtgk2%2FGroup%252078580%2520%281%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3aea36fe&sv=2)

# Setting up the SDK | Offerwall SDK

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk#id-1.-add-this-to-your-build.gradle-file)

1\. Add this to your build.gradle file

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your build.gradle file

Kotlin Script

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk#tab-kotlin-script)

Groovy

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk#tab-groovy)

Copy

    implementation('com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.6-beta1')

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.6-beta1'

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk#id-2.-clean-build-and-rebuild-the-project)

2\. Clean build and Rebuild the project

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/setting-up-the-sdk#id-3.-configure-proguard-rules)

3\. Configure proguard rules

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    
    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

---

# Initialize the SDK | Offerwall SDK

To initialize the SDK, call the PubscaleOfferwall.init() method.

Pass the app API key (generated from the console) as the first parameter of the init method. Make sure to call the init method as soon as your app starts up, ideally in app.js or index.js.

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#optional-parameters)

Optional Parameters:

**user\_id:** Pass your user's id in this field to tag your user. This id will be sent along with the S2S callback. Make sure to call the init function every time the user id changes.

**background\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed as a banner on top of the offer wall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. The background will be black by default.

**appicon\_Base64:** An image that will be displayed in the center on the top banner of the offerwall. Pass the image in base64 encoded format. Default value is the app icon.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/initialize-the-sdk#initializing-the-sdk)

Initializing the SDK

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Copy

    import {NativeModules, Alert} from 'react-native';
    const {PubscaleOfferwall} = NativeModules;
    
    //initialises the SDK.
    //call init once the user is logged in.
    
    PubscaleOfferwall.init( "APP_ID", {
        "user_id": "test-user", //optional, but require to tag user to offer completion.
        "background_Base64": base64Image,
        "appicon_Base64": app64Image, //optional
    }, () => { //onSuccess Callback
        console.log("success")
    }, (errMsg)=>{ //onFailure Callbacks
        console.log(errMsg)
    })

The SDK Initialization is complete. Learn how to launch the offerwall in the next step.

[PreviousSetting up the SDK](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk)
[NextStart the OfferWall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/start-the-offerwall)

# Setting up the SDK | Offerwall SDK

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-1.-add-this-to-your-build.gradle-file)

Add the below line inside the **dependencies** block in your build.gradle file

Kotlin Script

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#tab-kotlin-script)

Groovy

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#tab-groovy)

Copy

    implementation('com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.6-beta1')

Copy

    implementation 'com.pubscale.sdkone:offerwall:1.0.6-beta1'

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-2.-clean-build-and-rebuild-the-project)

2\. Clean build and Rebuild the project

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-3.-configure-proguard-rules)

3\. Configure proguard rules

For the SDK to work properly in release(obfuscated/minified) builds, add the following rules in your proguard-rules.pro file.

proguard-rules.pro

Copy

    -keep class com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.** {*;}
    #Supporting R8 full mode
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class kotlin.coroutines.Continuation
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking interface retrofit2.Call
    -keep,allowobfuscation,allowshrinking class retrofit2.Response
    

We have added the SDK to the project. Learn how to initialize the SDK in the next step

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-5.-add-native-module-files)

5\. Add native module files

Add the following files to your android app's module directory.

*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.java](https://storage.googleapis.com/pubscale-offerwall/lib/PubscaleOfferwallSdkModule.java)
    
*   [PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage.java](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1)
    

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/setting-up-the-sdk#id-6.-link-the-module)

6\. Link the module

Add the following line inside the getPackages() method of MainApplication class.

`packages.add(new PubscaleOfferwallSdkPackage());`

# Start the OfferWall | Offerwall SDK

To start the offerwall, just call, `OfferWall.launch(Context, OfferWallListener);`

A listener can be set to listen for events fired by the Offer Wall.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-kotlin)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-java)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallListener = object : OfferWallListener{
    
       override fun onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.")
       }
    
       override fun onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.")
       }
    
       override fun onRewardClaimed(reward: Reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.")
       }
    
       override fun onFailed(message: String) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: $message")
       }
    }                 

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.Reward
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallListener offerWallListener = new OfferWallListener() {
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallShowed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall showed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onOfferWallClosed() {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall closed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onRewardClaimed(@NonNull Reward reward) {
           Log.d(TAG, "Offer wall reward claimed.");
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onFailed(@NonNull String message) {
           Log.d(TAG, "onFailed: " + message);
       }
    };

onRewardClaimed callback gives you the reward amount and currency details.

To start the OfferWall, call the launch method of the OfferWall class.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-kotlin-1)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/start-the-offerwall#tab-java-1)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall
    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.models.OfferWallListener
    ..
    ..
    OfferWall.launch(context, offerWallListener)            

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWall

# Initialize the SDK | Offerwall SDK

You must initialize the SDK before using the SDK. To do this, call `Offerwall.init(OfferWallConfig, OfferWallInitListener)` .

Parameters for init call:

*   **OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig:** An object to pass configuration-related info to the SDK while initializing. Refer below for how to create an object of OfferWallConfig.
    
*   **OfferWallInitListener offerWallInitListener:** A listener that informs you if the SDK initialization was successful or not. In case of failure, it will also give you a string stating the cause of the failure. This parameter is optional.
    

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#creating-offerwallconfig-object)

**Creating OfferWallConfig object:**

Create an instance of OfferWallConfig using the builder class OfferWallConfig.Builder by passing the context and your PubScale app ID.

Use sandbox environment app ID for testing purposes.

[Sandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)
 - Learn how to setup Sandbox environment

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-kotlin)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-java)

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    val offerWallConfig = OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
       .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
       .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap) //optional
       .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foreground) //optional
       .setFullscreenEnabled(false) //optional
       .build()

Copy

    import com.pubscale.sdkone.offerwall.OfferWallConfig
    ..
    ..
    OfferWallConfig offerWallConfig =
           new OfferWallConfig.Builder(context, "YOUR_PUBSCALE_APP_ID")
                   .setUniqueId("unique_id") //optional, used to represent the user of your application
                   .setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(backgroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setLoaderForegroundBitmap(foregroundBitmap)//optional
                   .setFullscreenEnabled(false)//optional
                   .build();

These are the public methods available for OfferWallConfig.Builder class:

Public Methods

Description

setUniqueId(String uniqueId)

Sets a unique id that will be used to identify the user uniquely. This will be sent back in the postback.

setFullscreenEnabled(Boolean isEnabled)

Sets if the offerwall should open in fullscreen mode or not. Default: false

setLoaderBackgroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the background image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: Black color image

setLoaderForegroundBitmap(Bitmap bitmap)

Accepts a bitmap and uses it as the foreground image for the loader and offerwall top banner. Default: App icon

build()

Builds the config and returns OfferWallConfig instance

If a unique ID is not set, rewarding the user is not guaranteed.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#undefined-1)

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#initialize-the-offerwall-sdk)

**Initialize the Offerwall SDK:**

Initialize the OfferWall SDK by calling the init function by passing the offer wall config.

Kotlin

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-kotlin-1)

Java

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/native-android/initialize-the-sdk#tab-java-1)

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, object : OfferWallInitListener {
       override fun onInitSuccess() {
       }
       override fun onInitFailed(error: InitError) {
       }
    })

Copy

    OfferWall.init(offerWallConfig, new OfferWallInitListener() {
       @Override
       public void onInitSuccess() {
    
       }
    
       @Override
       public void onInitFailed(@NonNull InitError error) {
    
       }
    });

OfferWallInitListener is an optional parameter in init() method.

If you need to change any config after initializing the SDK, you should destroy and re-init the SDK.

To destroy, call `OfferWall.destroy()`

# S2S Callback Configuration | Offerwall SDK

You can configure the S2S callback for the offerwall in the dashboard inside the Offerwall's overview section.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-1.-setup-callback-url)

1\. Setup Callback URL

When a user has earned a reward by completing an offer, we fire an HTTP GET request to the provided callback URL. The following query parameters will be part of the request.

Copy

    <callback_url>?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>
          
    //Example http://www.example.com/payments/offers/pubscale?user_id=<user_id>&value=<value>&token=<token>&signature=<signature>

Query Params

Description

user\_id

The 'unique\_id' set while initializing the SDK.

value

The decimal value of the reward earned by the user.

token

A token that uniquely represents the transaction.

signature

Hash of the above values to verify the request (more info below).

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-2.-server-response)

2\. Server Response

Responding to the callback URL with status codes between and including the values 200 to 299 will mark the callback as successfully delivered.

In the event of the server not responding with any of the aforementioned status codes, the request will be **retried 6 times** at different intervals. You can utilize the unique token sent in the request to avoid rewarding the user multiple times for the same callback.

### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#id-3.-optional-parameters-for-fraud-detection-prevention)

3\. Optional Parameters for fraud detection/prevention

The value sent in the signature parameter can be used to validate the identity of the origin of the request. The value is an MD5 hash of the template below. The secret key is an additional key that will be provided along with the APP API KEY.

Golang

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-golang)

NodeJs

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-nodejs)

Python

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-python)

PHP

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#tab-php)

Copy

    
    template := fmt.Sprintf("%s.%s.%d.%s", <secret_key>, <user_id>, <int({value>), <token>)
    hash := toMD5(template)
    
      if hash != {signature} {
            return errors.New("invalid signature")
      }
    
    func toMD5(text string) string {
      algorithm := md5.New()
      algorithm.Write([]byte(text))
      return hex.EncodeToString(algorithm.Sum(nil))
    }
    

Copy

    
    const md5 = require('md5')
      
    const template = `${<secret_key>}.${<user_id>}.${Math.trunc(<value>)}.${<token>}`
    const hash = md5(template)
    
    if(signature != hash) {
        return false
    }
    

Copy

    
    import hashlib
    
    template = '{secret_key}.{user_id}.{value}.{token}'.format(secret_key=<secret_key>,user_id=<user_id>,value=int(<value>),token=<token>)
    hash = hashlib.md5(template.encode('utf-8')).hexdigest()
    
    if hash != <signature>:
        return false            
        

Copy

    function calculateHash() {
    	
    	$user = $_GET['user_id'];
    	$token = $_GET['token'];
    	$value = $_GET['value'];
    
    	$template = <secret_key>. "." . $user . "." . (int)$value . "." $token;
    
    	return calculateMD5($template);
    }
    
    function calculateMD5($data) {
    	return hash('md5', $data);
    }
    
    $hash = $_GET['signature'];
    
    if ($hash != calculateHash()) {
    	return false
    }

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#example)

Example

secret\_key = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13` user\_id = `30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD` value = `100.1234` token = `525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

Final format = `fa072672-d432-11c4-885a-EB1CdEc4Bb13.30356439-8d15-4f47-B133-010a37C19eBD.100.525a5B8e-512b-441A-a10B-72d218c370e5`

#### 

[](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/s2s-callback-configuration/s2s-callback-configuration#steps-to-validate-the-value-of-the-hash)

Steps to validate the value of the hash

1.  Concatenate the values in the above format.
    
2.  Make sure to convert the value parameter from decimal to integer.
    
3.  Calculate the MD5 hash of the concatenated value.
    
4.  Build Hex encode of the generated value.
    
5.  Verify if the calculated value is equal to the value sent in the signature parameter.
    

As the value of the secret key will only be known to you and PubScale’s server, the hash cannot be generated by a fraudulent third party.

[PreviousStart the OfferWall](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/react-native/start-the-offerwall)
[NextSandbox Environment](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/1.0.6-beta1/sandbox-environment/sandbox-environment)

# Sandbox Environment | Offerwall SDK

Sandbox environment enables you to test out the integration before you release your app. You will be able to test the complete integration starting from initializing the SDK to getting callbacks.

Also, any changes in the sandbox environment do not affect the production environment.

1.  **Switch to the sandbox environment using the toggle in the dashboard**
    

Switching to the Sandbox environment in the dashboard does not affect your production environment.

![](https://pubscale.gitbook.io/offerwall-sdk/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4187661493-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcJjYVtSXK83YJkG3H9nv%252Fuploads%252FvwyCRD1eA0mzGhRN5z3i%252FGroup%252078582.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D856a568f-7127-46a6-9444-1f0c98388fab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4df842b8&sv=2)

Sandbox Environment toggle

1.  **Copy the app ID shown for the sandbox environment and use it in the app**
    
2.  **Additionally, you can also configure a different S2S callback for your sandbox environment by clicking on the Configure Callback button in the sandbox environment.**
